1935.10.21

England Reaffirms Six Articles: Supporting the Covenant to Eliminate Warfare, Unwilling to Act Alone, European Situation Slightly Clarified 1

(London) British Ambassador to Rome, Sir Eric Drummond, recently held talks with Italian Prime Minister Mussolini and reiterated Britain's stance on the Italo-Abyssinian dispute. According to a Foreign Office statement issued today, Sir Drummond visited the Italian Prime Minister on Friday and reiterated that Britain, apart from the collective obligations incumbent upon a loyal member of the League of Nations, or those decided by the League of Nations in accordance with the provisions of the Covenant, is unwilling to take separate action and explained that Britain's attitude towards this case is not for its own benefit. All rumors are baseless and are spread by those who mistranslate the news or gloat over disasters. Rome also issued a similar statement. (Reuters, 20th)

(Rome) The situation of Prime Minister Mussolini's talk with British Ambassador Sir Eric Drummond yesterday has been announced. Sir Eric Drummond again assured the Prime Minister that Britain, with the status of a faithful member of the League of Nations, undertakes collective obligations, and apart from the actions taken to fulfill these obligations and the actions recommended by the League of Nations in accordance with the Covenant, Britain is unwilling to take separate action, and stated that Britain's stance on the Italo-Abyssinian dispute is not related to its own interests. (Havas, 19th)

Rome Expresses Satisfaction

(Rome) According to officials, after British Ambassador Sir Eric Drummond explained Britain's attitude to Prime Minister Mussolini yesterday, the Italian government and people expressed their satisfaction, believing that the two countries will be more understanding in the future. The purpose of Drummond's visit was to clarify the situation in the Mediterranean, and now the situation there has indeed eased. Britain and Italy will continue to hold talks. Officials believe that Sir Drummond may not have made concrete proposals yesterday, but both sides have the possibility of reaching a solution. (Havas, 20th)

British-Italian Continued Talks

(London) Foreign Secretary Sir Samuel Hoare recently held secret talks with Italian Ambassador Count Grandi, and jointly considered the issue of withdrawing a portion of the Italian troops stationed in Libya, Africa, and the recall of two British warships, HMS Renown and HMS Hotham, from the Strait of Gibraltar to their home country. Generally, since the French government has agreed to provide assistance once the British Navy is attacked in the Mediterranean, the British move to recall warships is quite possible. According to sources from this agency, Britain will not demand that Italy withdraw all its troops stationed in Libya, but will request them to be moved away from the Egyptian border. In addition, Hoare and Grandi also discussed Italy's minimum conditions for peace. It is heard that these peace talks will proceed as quickly as possible, because Mussolini has said that if the Italian army continues to advance, the conditions put forward by Italy will increase accordingly. It is generally believed that when an international trusteeship system is established in the Abyssinian province of Ogaden and its headquarters in the future (referring to the League of Nations' mandate), difficulties will arise if Italy insists on occupying a superior position, but those in charge are optimistic about the general situation of the current negotiations. (Havas, 19th)

Consolidation of International Position

(London) Diplomatic circles believe that the peace talks among Britain, France, and Italy have greatly consolidated the position of the League of Nations and have eliminated obstacles to cooperation between Britain and France in Geneva. Rumors say that Italian Prime Minister Mussolini has expressed the minimum conditions for peace to British and French representatives. (National Telegraph, 19th)

Baldwin's Speech: Britain Voluntarily Promotes Peace 2

(London) British Prime Minister Baldwin said in a speech in Worcester this afternoon that Britain has not taken separate action in the conflict between the League of Nations and Italy, and will not do so in the future. The League of Nations and the Kellogg-Briand Pact have failed to eliminate war, and Britain has to bear the responsibility of finding ways to end the war and restore peace, but Britain has not taken separate action in this regard. War is the most unwanted thing in the minds of the British government. The British government is always prepared to use any opportunity as a member of the League of Nations to seek peace. Some say that Britain's actions are aimed at overthrowing the Italian fascist system, which is the most harmful slander. The Prime Minister finally made an important statement about himself, saying, "I hope in my heart that I will never compete in the general election again, but I will wait and see about not competing in the election in the future. The general election after this one may be some time away. I only decided yesterday that the general election should not be delayed any longer and must be held as soon as possible." (Reuters, 19th)

Italian Policy: Diplomacy and Military Advance Together, Resisting League of Nations Sanctions While Continuing to Deploy Troops to East Africa 3

(Rome) According to a telegram from this agency's interviewer, after the activities of the British, French, and Italian governments in diplomacy in recent days, important figures in the political circles here believe that Italy's views on the Abyssinian war and the League of Nations' sanctions have not been swayed. The things that should be paid attention to now are three items: (1) Since British Ambassador Sir Eric Drummond met with Prime Minister Mussolini, Britain will certainly not take separate action against Italy, but collective intervention is still possible. Regarding the Italo-Abyssinian dispute, Britain can still intervene in accordance with the wishes of the League of Nations, and Italy is afraid that it will urge the League of Nations to issue an intervention order, so it should continue to send troops to East Africa and prepare to resist the League of Nations' sanctions. (2) Since the League of Nations has forced its member states to boycott Italian goods, it still allows these countries to continue to import goods into Italy, except for those used in war. In this regard, Italy can only take retaliatory measures against countries that implement sanctions, that is, prohibit the import of goods from these countries into Italy. (3) Italy is still willing to clarify its relationship with the League of Nations. Regarding this, Italy's chief representative to the League of Nations, Mr. Aloisi, issued a statement saying that Italy's actions against Abyssinia are in line with the principles contained in the League of Nations Covenant, and it is very possible to prove it. Seeing that the people of the Abyssinian province of Tigray welcome the Italian army, abolish the slave system, and correct the anarchic state of the border provinces of Abyssinia, we know that the actions of the Italian government are fully justified. In other words, (A) Italy is not an aggressor but a liberator, (B) Abyssinia's promotion of the slave system should not be on an equal footing with civilized countries, (C) Abyssinia's so-called unity is artificial. Officials also believe that if the League of Nations reconsiders the Italo-Abyssinian dispute based on the actual situation, then the relationship between Italy and the League of Nations will not be difficult to clarify. (Havas, 20th)

Leader of Italian Veterans Visits London: Task to Probe Public Opinion and Eliminate Misunderstandings, Denying Formal Mission 4

(London) General Garibaldi, leader of Italian veterans and friend of Prime Minister Mussolini (grandson of the Italian founding hero), recently arrived here from Rome. It is rumored that Garibaldi's trip is to try to collect British public opinion so that he can have a basis for resolving the Italo-Abyssinian dispute in the future. Officials have denied this, and Garibaldi himself also made a statement to the Sunday Chronicle to defend himself, saying, "I have not been entrusted with a formal mission here, but my mother is British, and I also believe in the English Orthodox Church. I may be able to clarify the misunderstandings of Italy by Britain in recent weeks. Italy is not preparing for war, nor does it want to engage in war, nor has it ever sought war before, but one thing that can make Italians feel unhappy is that Britain is taking separate action. Our Prime Minister Mussolini has guaranteed that British interests are sacred and will never be violated. I don't know why the British government requires France to provide assistance in the Mediterranean. Regarding the Abyssinian issue, Italy is prepared to discuss it fully within or outside the League of Nations. What we hope from other countries is to be open and honest and not to act rashly before understanding Italy's views." (Havas, 20th)

British Representative Eden Leaves Geneva for Home, Briefly Stopping in Paris 5

(Geneva) The British representative, Minister for League of Nations Affairs Anthony Eden, set off for home at 11 p.m. tonight and will arrive in Paris tomorrow, where he will stay for a few hours to meet with League of Nations Secretary-General Avenol. (Havas, 19th)

(Paris) British Under-Secretary of State Anthony Eden arrived here from Geneva at 8:15 this morning and rushed to London at 10:30. (Havas, 20th)

League of Nations Sanctions Committee Decides: Steps to Universally Boycott Italian Goods, Maintaining Justice with Willingness to Sacrifice, Calling on Non-Member States to Participate in Cooperation, Austro-Hungarian Representatives Opposed and Criticized 6

(Geneva) The 52-member Sanctions Coordination Committee held a plenary meeting yesterday and made an important resolution to universally boycott Italian goods in an atmosphere of quiet discussion. The steps taken are as follows: (1) Adopted the British representative Anthony Eden's proposal to boycott Italian exports. (2) Unanimously supported the proposal regarding the organization of a mutual assistance committee. (3) Passed a proposal to prohibit the import of certain items into Italy. The list of prohibited items was passed on the spot. Austria and Hungary abstained from voting on the first proposal, and in addition to Austria and Hungary, Albania was also unwilling to vote on the third proposal. The representatives of Austria and Hungary all reiterated their reasons for opposing the sanctions and not voting, which were based on economic damage, but the broad resolution of the 52-member committee, despite the opposition of Austria and Hungary, can greatly represent international solidarity. Its most important characteristic is the willingness and spirit of self-sacrifice. Small countries also have this willingness and, with this spirit, are prepared to accept the losses caused by the sanctions. This resolution will have a disturbing effect on Italy. Although the actual impact of the sanctions cannot be predicted now, the spiritual impact is definitely not small. Soviet representative Litvinov made an important statement, saying that Soviet trade with Italy is in a surplus, but he is prepared to suffer losses to fulfill his obligations, but other countries must also abide by this obligation. If exceptional actions invalidate the sanctions, the Soviet Union will have to reconsider its overall position and make new decisions. The issue of non-member states participating in sanctions against Italy was also discussed by the committee in a closed-door meeting. The chairman stated that the most important issue that has always been on his mind but has not been resolved is the status of non-member states. He asked non-member states to maintain the dignity of the law over force with moral concepts and to prevent aggression in international life. Although they are not member states, they are signatories to the Paris Peace Pact. The League of Nations should inform all non-member states of its actions and proposals for handling the Italo-Abyssinian dispute and ask them to express their opinions. He believes that now is the time. To what extent can our suggestions serve a common purpose, and how should non-member states take the same actions as us to cooperate? These questions, we can only let each non-member state decide according to its conscience. At the afternoon meeting of the Sanctions Coordination Committee, the attitude of Austria and Hungary was widely criticized. Romanian representative Titulescu spoke passionately, saying that the imports of these two countries should be banned as a warning to those who do not comply with the sanctions. Then he talked about the most-favored-nation treatment clause, and the debate was very fierce, but it was later decided not to mention non-member states in its resolution. The Mutual Assistance Committee met yesterday, and one notable feature of its report was that it decided not to allow Austria and Hungary to increase their imports, and they should be held responsible, that is, in terms of exports, they should also suffer the same degree of loss as the countries participating in the sanctions. The next meeting of the Sanctions Coordination Committee will be held on October 31, when the date for the implementation of the sanctions will be decided. (Reuters, 20th)

Full Text of Mutual Assistance Plan: Compensating Losses Incurred by Sanctions, Resolution Passed by the Coordination Committee 7

(Geneva) The Sanctions Plan Coordination Committee recently passed a resolution to adopt mutual assistance measures in accordance with Article 16, paragraph 3 of the Covenant. The full text is as follows: The governments of the member states of the League of Nations should, under the existing obligations, consider various measures:

(1) To increase the number of seaports in each country by various appropriate means, so that countries participating in sanctions that have lost the markets of member states can benefit. (2) If certain member states do not participate in sanctions and benefit from the implementation of sanctions by other member states, each member state should compare the mutual assistance obligations that these countries should bear with the benefits they have obtained, and take appropriate measures within a reasonable range to reduce the number of imported goods in these countries in order to offset them. (3) Countries participating in sanctions should try to encourage companies that usually specialize in exporting certain goods to Italy to increase their mutual trade with companies that usually specialize in importing such goods due to losses caused by sanctions. (4) Countries participating in sanctions should jointly organize a trade system to offset the loss of the Italian market due to participation in sanctions. (5) If the measures taken in trade cannot have a considerable effect on mutual assistance, then the countries participating in sanctions should consider the possibility of taking financial measures.

The Coordination Committee then passed a suggestion put forward by Romanian representative Titulescu and decided to implement special sanction measures against member states who refuse to participate in sanctions against Italy, namely Austria and Hungary. Titulescu's proposal was supported by Britain, Russia, the Little Entente, and the Balkan Entente. Mr. Conducis (Spain) of the Economic Mutual Assistance Committee once issued a statement, "The measures taken by the League of Nations to protect international law, each non-member state has the power to facilitate or reduce its effectiveness." This statement was aimed at Japan, the United States, Brazil, and Germany, four non-member states. Conducis suggested that since these countries are signatories to the Non-Aggression Pact, the League of Nations may send a copy of the results of its work and the text of various resolutions to the governments of these countries. If these countries believe that it is necessary to raise opinions on the sanctions issue, please notify him. This suggestion was passed by the Coordination Committee. (Havas, 19th)

Eighteen-Nation Group Postpones Meeting

(Geneva) The eighteen-nation small-scale committee announced the postponement of the meeting until after October 21. Spokespersons for the British and Russian delegations both said to this agency's interviewer, "The cooperation between Britain and France is closely related to European peace." The spokesperson for the British delegation also expressed the hope that the cooperation between Britain and France can make the League of Nations Covenant a complete victory. "Conversely, if Britain and France cannot cooperate, then Britain does not intend to take separate action, and it is better to stay out of it. The impact of this is probably beyond what can be expected." (Havas, 19th)

Italy Expresses No Fear

(Rome) A semi-official Italian newspaper said that Italy is quite capable of resisting economic sanctions. "In 1934, Italy purchased more than 30% of its total imports from Japan, Brazil, the United States, and Germany. The goods purchased from Austria and Hungary accounted for 3.7% of the total imports. Japan, Brazil, the United States, and Germany are not member states of the League of Nations. Once economic sanctions are implemented, the goods they supply to Italy will inevitably increase. Among them, Germany accounts for about 40% of the coal needed by Italy, and Britain accounts for 39%." The newspaper also said that in 1934, Italy imported industrial products worth 1,541,000,000 lire. It is now planned to stop purchasing them and replace them with domestic products. Italy is actively researching new manufacturing methods. (Havas, 19th)

Italy's Bank Reserves Decrease

(Rome) From the 30th of last month to the 10th of this month, the gold reserves of the National Bank of Italy decreased by 226,000,000 lire to 4,025,354,000 lire. Foreign currency reserves increased from 392,533,000 lire to 412,644,000 lire. The amount of paper money in circulation increased from 15,271,716,000 lire to 15,425,510,000 lire. (Havas, 19th)

US Attitude to Be Considered

(Washington) According to State Department officials today, after the League of Nations' document requesting non-member states to universally boycott Italian goods is delivered, the US government will consider its attitude towards this move. However, the officials believe that the United States currently has no laws to prohibit the import of Italian goods. According to the Neutrality Act, any trade restriction must be applied to both belligerent countries, but Abyssinia's trade with the United States is minimal. This regulation is enough to have a significant impact on Italy. (Reuters, 20th)

Abyssinian King Firmly States: Vows Not to Give Up an Inch of Land, No Peace Talks Unless Italian Troops Withdraw, Trust in League of Nations Remains Consistent 8

(Berlin) The Abyssinian Emperor said to an interviewer from the Nazi Party's organ newspaper, the People's Observer, yesterday, "A fair and honorable peace treaty is indeed what we desire, but as long as a part of Abyssinian land is occupied by Italian troops, we will not conduct negotiations with Italy. Although we cherish peace, in the current situation, there is no possibility of proposing peace talks. The entire issue is now in the hands of the League of Nations, and only the League of Nations has the right to seek a solution. We have previously considered reducing the border line and exchanging land in accordance with the spirit of reciprocity, but if we cannot obtain compensation and abandon the land, then we have never considered it. This method will only make the two countries the only victims and is definitely not acceptable to us." (Havas, 19th)

Abyssinian Army Concentrated at Southern Key Points, King's Son-in-Law Directs at the Front Line, Ample Military Supplies Hinder Enemy Progress 9

Abyssinian Capital: According to official announcements, the Abyssinian army is still completing its military plans, which are sufficient to resist the Italian army's attack. At present, the Italian army's progress has been curbed by the Abyssinian outpost line. The Abyssinian army is in a strategically favorable position. (Havas, 19th)

(Rome) The Abyssinian army is now moving in the Italian Somaliland border area, and its intention seems to be to prevent the Italian army there from contacting the Eritrean army. People here are paying close attention to this matter, because General Graziani (commander of Italian Somaliland) has established a strong base in Gelogubi in southern Abyssinia, from which he plans to launch a full-scale attack on Jijiga (east of Harar) to form a unified front with the Italian army in Eritrea. According to the results of Italian military aircraft inspections of the Abyssinian front line and the descriptions of prisoners, the Abyssinian army is concentrating in Geroe, which is located on the Fafan River and is the hub of the four major north-south and east-west thoroughfares. In terms of water conservancy and military strategy, it is the most important location in southern Ogaden province. The army led by Abyssinian General Nasibu is advancing from the north along the Fafan River towards Geroe. The required military supplies are transported from the Abyssinian capital to Harar province by truck, and then transported by donkeys. In addition, the official and unofficial army led by Chief Desdu of the Sidamo and Borana provinces will also head to Geroe to support General Nasibu. General Desdu is the king's son-in-law and claims to be able to summon 120,000 people to fight a desperate battle with the Italian army. He also has Belgian instructors to assist the army. In addition, the Sidamo and Borana provinces are located at the southern end of Abyssinia and are connected to Italian Somaliland and British Fania. Recently, a public road has been built to Kenya, so a large number of military supplies may have been received. (Havas, 19th)

Famous French European War General Talks: Italian Army Has Difficulty Winning, Abyssinia's Advantages in Geography and Endurance, Current Weapons Lose Their Effectiveness 10

(Paris) Army General Franchet d'Esperey, who served as the commander-in-chief of the Allied forces in Eastern Europe during the European War, had years of experience fighting in the mountainous and marshy areas of the Balkan Peninsula and the Vardar River (in Serbia), and finally defeated the allied forces of Bulgaria, Austria, and Hungary. Therefore, he has rich experience in wars in mountainous and marshy areas. He recently gave a speech at a banquet of the National Professional Groups Association, discussing Abyssinian military affairs, saying that he does not take sides with the belligerent countries, but from a military point of view, the Italian army will be able to achieve victory after taking large-scale military actions. He then recalled the defeat of the Italian army in the Battle of Adwa in 1896, saying that since occupying the city on the 5th of this month, the shame of defeat has been washed away. In addition, the Abyssinian regime has not been concentrated in the central government, and the weapons used by the country are old-fashioned. Generally, people do not know how to use modern automatic military equipment that determines victory in war. Abyssinian soldiers are also not very well educated, but Abyssinian soldiers are familiar with geography, and they know every hill and creek. Their actions can make armies with modern weapons feel dangerous. In addition, life is simple, and food and transportation are not a problem, so actions are more agile. Moreover, they are accustomed to the hot climate and life on the plateau and are most able to endure hardship. All of these are the strengths of the Abyssinian army. After the general finished his speech, the professional groups association discussed the current situation as usual. The issue discussed on this day was the Italo-Abyssinian war. (Havas, 20th)

Commentary

Welcome Mr. Dern, U.S. Secretary of War 11

— Star

The United States government recognizes the official establishment of the Philippine Commonwealth Government on November 15th, marking a new era in Far Eastern relations. Both the Congressional and Presidential branches have dispatched their top leaders to participate in person in Manila. Secretary of War Dern arrived in Shanghai today and will travel to Nanjing tomorrow to meet with leaders of our government. Following Mr. Dern's arrival in the East are former Chief of Staff General MacArthur, Vice President and Senate President Garner, the Speaker of the House, and several leaders of the Congressional Democratic Party. Before arriving in Shanghai, Mr. Dern spent several days in Japan, where he engaged in numerous exchanges with government leaders and prominent figures from all walks of life. At a time when relations between China, Japan, the England, and the United States are undergoing new developments, and when various Far Eastern issues urgently need a comprehensive solution, the Secretary of War, who bears the heavy responsibility of U.S. national defense and manages the Philippine Islands, has personally crossed the ocean to the East to exchange views. This will undoubtedly make an important contribution to this difficult situation. Taking this opportunity to witness the achievements of China's new construction and understand the aspirations of the Chinese people will further benefit the friendship between the traditionally friendly China and the United States. This is why we extend our sincere welcome to Mr. Dern. In terms of Mr. Dern's duties, he should have a deep understanding and make active efforts regarding Far Eastern issues. Although the U.S. Secretary of War is a civilian, he is legally responsible for the full implementation of the National Defense Act of 1920 and has the authority to manage the internal affairs of the Philippine Islands and Puerto Rico. The duties of the U.S. War Department are extremely diverse, ranging from military education, war plans, coastal defense, air defense, military law and supplies, to hydraulic engineering and the administration of the Panama Canal Zone, all of which are under the jurisdiction of the War Department. Although various duties are separately handled by the Chief of Staff, Chief Engineer, territorial governors, etc., the Secretary of War is responsible for overseeing the overall picture and supervising its implementation. The Philippine Islands are known to be the weakest link in the U.S. national defense chain. After autonomy, within ten years, the United States has lost most of its power to interfere in its internal affairs, but still bears full responsibility for its defense. This is because the U.S. flag has not been lowered, and U.S. naval ports still exist in Manila. If unfortunate events occur in the Philippines, whether internally or externally, it will involve the entire U.S. defense plan. Those in charge of military affairs must not only consider preventing enemy invasion but also prevent the occurrence of war before it happens. How to prevent the Philippines from becoming a powder keg in East Asia and how to make East Asian peace slightly more stable is what those who hold the reins of power should pay attention to. We believe that Mr. Dern's inspection and discussions will definitely make a contribution.

Secondly, in terms of Mr. Dern's life experience, he should have a deep understanding and make active contributions to China's silver problem. He was born 63 years ago and studied at the University of Nebraska in the West. At the young age of 23, he engaged in mining. For 20 years, he served as the manager of gold mines in Utah. In 1915, he entered politics and served as the governor of that state for eight years. Utah is the central region of silver mines. Silver senators in Congress, such as Mr. King and Mr. Thomas, all came from this state. Silver faction senators only know that increasing the price of silver can bring temporary benefits to silver mine capitalists and the people in silver mine regions, but they often ignore the poison that silver purchase policies have planted overseas. Mr. Dern has a full understanding of the wishes of the people in the silver mining region. He can take advantage of this trip to get an accurate impression and understanding of the resentment of the Chinese people towards the U.S. silver policy. The silver policy has shaken China's economic order and caused regrettable phenomena in Sino-U.S. relations. Mr. Dern is one of President Roosevelt's most trusted people and one of the most powerful leaders of the Democratic Party. He should know to make suggestions to harmonize U.S. foreign policy, economic policy, national defense plan, and foreign trade plan.

The current situation in the Far East is quite severe. The United States either advances or retreats, with no possibility of hesitation. After the outbreak of the war between Italy and Ethiopia, alarming events have occurred in the Shantou and Hankou areas. Judging from the U.S. warships sailing to Swatow, it is impossible for the United States to completely avoid being involved if something happens in the Far East. Preventing major disasters before they happen is the commendable quality of a statesman. We dare to express this wish on the day we welcome Mr. Dern's visit to China. We wonder what this wise guest thinks.

Concrete Implementation of Sino-Japanese Economic Cooperation: Japanese Government Approves Establishment of Xingzhong Company as the Central Organization for Developing North China's Industry 12

Wang Kemin and Others Fete Mantetsu Director Ishimoto, East Asia Economic Association Established in Tianjin Yesterday

(Beiping) Japan's proposal to establish the Xingzhong Company in Tianjin or Beiping for developing North China's industry has been approved by the Japanese government. It is learned that after the close of the Dalian Conference, the opinions of the Japanese Army Central Department and the local organizations have become consistent, and the opportunity for Sino-Japanese economic cooperation has become increasingly stronger. When Okamura, the second director of the Japanese General Staff Headquarters, arrived in Tianjin this time, he further confirmed that the Xingzhong Company should be established as the central organization for developing North China's industry. Okamura also suggested to Mantetsu President Matsuoka Yosuke in writing, and Matsuoka replied with a telegram expressing his agreement. It is expected that the establishment can be implemented in early next month, and then the company will start various economic tasks. (20th Dispatch)

(Beiping) Wang Kemin and Tang Erhe will host a banquet at the Beijing Hotel tonight for Ishimoto, a director of Japan's South Manchuria Railway (Mantetsu), and will invite important military and political figures, as well as Takahashi, a military attaché from the Japanese Embassy, to accompany them. (20th Dispatch)

(Tianjin) The so-called Far East Economic Association held its establishment ceremony this afternoon at a certain hotel in the Japanese Concession. (Tokyo) The Xingzhong Company, the organization for economic work in China that has now been decided to be established, has been discussing its functions with the South Manchuria Railway (Mantetsu) Affairs Bureau of the Army and Navy for days. League of Nations Work Situation: Committee on Mandates Reviews Annual Reports from Various Regions, Germany's Withdrawal from the League Takes Effect Today 13

(Geneva) The League of Nations' organs related to health, drug control, and mandates have also been meeting in Geneva in the past few days. The Health Committee passed a report on Tuesday last week on conducting research on venereal disease tumors, epilepsy, and malaria. The committee also began to research nutritional products in accordance with the recent proposals of the League of Nations, and to study construction from the aspects of health, heating, ventilation, sunlight, and electricity. The Opium Supervision Committee prepared a report on Saturday last week explaining the estimated quantities of dangerous drugs needed by 179 countries and regions next year. The Committee on Mandates held its 28th meeting on the 19th to review the annual reports of Cameroon, Togo, Ruanda-Urundi, Western Samoa, and the Pacific Islands under Japanese mandate. Germany remitted approximately 5 million francs to the League of Nations on Wednesday last week to cover its share of this year's League expenses and previous arrears. Since Germany has fulfilled its financial obligations, its membership in the League of Nations will cease on Monday next week (i.e., the 21st of this month). (19th Central News Agency Dispatch)

Torrential Slumping, Huangdi Embankment in Lengzhai Continues to Collapse 24

(Tianjin) Baoding telephone, Hebei Provincial Government received a telegram from Li Qingping, the Huanghe River supervision commissioner, stating that the beaches and embankments in the Lengzhai area at the junction of the 3rd and 4th sections in the south are collapsing more severely due to the continuous surging of the river for several days. The No. 1 and No. 2 dikes have each subsided four or five feet since the top was hit by the great surging on the 14th evening. After all-night rescue efforts, they were stabilized at noon on the 16th. However, the surging continued and the collapsing continued. A brick dike was built on top of the first dike, and two willow dikes were built. Currently, the bottom is being paved and net-casting and brick-throwing are being carried out to resist. The newly built brick dike at the 12th shop of the 2nd section in the south was severely submerged by the impact of the great surging. The funds and materials are all lacking. The brick households are not moving forward because the transportation fees have not been paid. The office wall of the section has been demolished and the bricks are being temporarily used. (20th Dispatch)

(Tianjin) Baoding telephone, Qi Shou'an, director of the Yellow River Affairs Bureau, telegraphed the province, stating that the No. 1 and No. 2 water diversion dikes at the first shop collapsed and subsided by several tens of feet each due to the scouring of the surging river on the evening of the 14th to the morning of the 15th. Division Chief He supervised the civilians to block the breach for several days. The surging river at Liu Zhuang is still directly impacting the east dike. The 5th section of the 5th and 9th sweepstakes were all seen to be sinking. Soil is currently being pressed on the 9th sweepstake to protect the roots of the 8th sweepstake. (20th Dispatch)

Donghai is located downstream of Shuyang and Guannan, and the water situation is very dangerous. County Mayor He Zhengang plans to abandon the second line of defense and rush to build the third waterproof line for defense. However, because the sacrifice after abandoning it is too great, it will not be retreated unless it is absolutely necessary. (20th Dispatch)

Italy's Armed Forces Reach 1.2 Million, One-Sixth Sent to East Africa, Decision to Continue Enlistment of New Recruits 55

(Rome) Although Italy's armed forces have reached 1.2 million men, it has been decided to continue enlisting new recruits. Reservists from the 1911 to 1914 classes, including those previously exempt from military service, are now being conscripted, and mobilization orders have been issued for the 1915 class. Soldiers from the 1911, 1913, and 1914 classes will be retained for indefinite service. The semi-official Italian newspaper views the aforementioned steps as a response to the untrustworthy remarks made by French General Weygand, who stated that Italy's military strength had been greatly reduced due to the Abyssinian war and could no longer be considered a military power. The newspaper also stated that of Italy's 1.2 million armed men, only 200,000 are in the colonies. (20th Reuters dispatch)

Three steamships, the "Hairano," "Sardinia," and "Egnazia," carrying several thousand sappers, guards, gendarmes, and many reconnaissance and bomber aircraft, departed yesterday afternoon for the Italian colony of Eritra in East Africa. The steamship "Ambruria," carrying 2,000 machine gunners and technicians, as well as many ambulances, departed for Italian Somaliland. In addition, the steamships "Sicilia," "Lombardia," and "Calabria" are scheduled to depart on Sunday, carrying over 8,000 soldiers to the port of Massawa. (20th Havas dispatch)

Commander-in-Chief of Italian Forces in East Africa Issues Ultimatum, Demanding Allegiance from Chiefs Within Ten Days 56

(Rome) According to the Roman newspaper "Il Popolo di Roma," General Tabloni, Commander-in-Chief of Italian forces in East Africa, has issued an ultimatum to the chiefs of Tigray and Agame in Abyssinia, demanding their surrender within ten days, after which they will be considered enemies. (20th Reuters dispatch)

Imperial Proclamation to Reassure the People

(Rome) General Tabloni, High Commissioner of Italian East Africa, has issued a proclamation in Italian and Tigrinya to the residents of Tigray and Asmara, which has been posted in the towns and villages of the Italian-occupied areas. It states, in essence: "Residents of Tigray and Agame, from today onwards, you are under Italian jurisdiction and protection. Tribal chiefs, remain in your positions and be responsible for the order and discipline of your areas. Within ten days, you must surrender to the nearest Italian authorities together with the clergy in your territories, otherwise you will be considered enemies. Anyone who has suffered losses due to the war may apply for compensation from the military commanders. All excessive taxes are abolished. People of agriculture and commerce, live in peace and work diligently." The Italian government has donated 15,000 thalers (Abyssinian currency) to the Coptic Church in Aksum. (19th Havas dispatch)

Abolition of Slavery

A front-line correspondent for this agency in Tigray reports that General Tabloni, High Commissioner of Italian East Africa, has issued an order abolishing slavery. It states, "Wherever the Italian flag flies, there is freedom. You have always known this. From now on, all forms of slavery in your country are strictly prohibited. All slaves in Tigray are now free, and the slave trade is also prohibited. Anyone who violates this decree will be punished severely for disobeying government orders." (20th Havas dispatch)

Suffering Greatly from Water Shortage, Italian Soldiers Falling Ill Repeatedly 57

Suez: The Italian troops in East Africa are experiencing a severe water shortage. The many wells dug inland and in the mountains contain salty water, unsuitable for drinking and only usable for washing. All troop carriers are now carrying as much water as possible to alleviate this shortage. Food for the soldiers is also a serious problem. Abyssinian soldiers do not suffer from the lack of water because they all have fruits and vegetables in their bags, which they can eat to quench their thirst for a long time without drinking water. Italian soldiers are falling ill repeatedly, suffering from fever, joint pain, pneumonia, kidney disease, and dysentery. Two Italian ships are now dedicated to making ice in Massawa for the sick. Sappers with rifles are working behind the lines, as hard as the soldiers on the front lines. Many of them have petitioned General Tabloni, the Commander-in-Chief, to allow them to go to the front to fight instead of building roads. The Commander-in-Chief consoled them, saying that building roads is also a path to glory. The gasoline stored in Eritrea is limited and is being used up quickly. The Italian army is finding it difficult to replenish its supply because the Suez refineries refuse to extend credit. The Italian army is now buying as many trucks as possible in Suez, even old ones, and shipping them to Massawa. (North-China Daily News, 19th special dispatch)

Violating International Agreements, Italian Army Uses Dumdum Bullets, Abyssinia Prepares to Protest to League of Nations 58

Addis Ababa: It has been reliably learned today that the Abyssinian government is preparing to protest to the League of Nations, claiming that the Italian army is using dumdum bullets, violating international agreements and Red Cross principles. These bullets reportedly cause massive wounds of up to twenty square inches when they enter the bodies of Abyssinian soldiers. The Abyssinian government will also protest the Italian army's bombing of cities without military installations, killing babies, and will vehemently deny Rome's claims that the Abyssinian army is using dumdum bullets. (19th National Ray)

Inner Mongolian Puppet Conference, Japanese Use Intimidation Tactics, Claiming Disputes Will Be Resolved by Force, but Outer Mongolian Representatives Remain Unmoved 60

(Moscow) A dispatch from Kulun reports news from Manzhouli: the Japanese representative at the Manchurian-Mongolian conference, Ganji (transliteration), is using fresh diplomatic tactics, breaking his own record. Ganji visited the other Mongolian representatives Dussen and Dangba without visiting the chief Mongolian representative, Sambo. With his usual threatening attitude, he forcefully ordered the Mongolian delegation to change its decisions. He said that if the Mongolian side did not accept the Manchurian side's suggestions, then the Manchurian side would have to use "other means," at which point there would be "serious incidents" on the border. At the same time, if the Mongolian Republic did not submit, all kinds of disputes "would be dealt with by force, not by peaceful means." However, these methods of the Japanese diplomat did not have the slightest effect on the Mongolian representatives. They remained calm and did not change their original intentions because of these rash threats. Seeing that his efforts were unsuccessful, Ganji then claimed that he had been ordered by the government to notify the Mongolian delegation that if they did not accept the Japanese-Manchurian suggestions, then the Japanese-Manchurian delegations "would go to the capital of the Mongolian Republic, Kulun, with their troops to forcefully resolve this issue." This method of negotiation is unprecedented in national defense talks. All circles in Kulun are extremely indignant about this and sincerely hope that the Japanese government can restore its rash and disruptive "diplomatic personnel" to normalcy. (20th TASS dispatch)

Western Journey: Observations and Experiences 67

— Chronicle

New Atmosphere in Sichuan

Starting upstream from Yichang, it takes four days to reach Chongqing by boat. Passing through the Three Gorges, the scenery on both banks is majestic and beautiful, with steep cliffs and rapid streams. The rivers and mountains are like a painting, and one's heart feels refreshed, instantly filled with boundless vitality. At four o'clock in the afternoon on the 29th, we passed Tieguang Cliff. After Tieguang Cliff is Que Shi Town, located on the right bank of the river, belonging to Sichuan Province, and is the border between Hubei and Sichuan provinces. Not far past Beishi, there is a bridge called "Wu Duo," which is quite humorous, presumably meaning that everyone should not grab territory. According to a friend on the same boat, this area was Yang Sen's defense zone in the early years of the Republic of China. This bridge was built during Yang Sen's troops' garrison. The traces of the defense zone system era still remain. After entering Sichuan Province, the soil gradually becomes fertile, appearing deep brown. The mountains are covered with crops or forests. Farmers work in the rain, and the fields are neatly arranged, showing the diligence of the people of Sichuan. Along the riverbanks, there are many碉楼 (fortified watchtowers), one built every few tens of feet. Most are built of mud, and some are still under construction. Nearby the watchtowers, it is said that a small number of troops are stationed. In case of bandits, the watchtowers communicate with each other to prevent bandits from entering. The Sichuan authorities are taking great pains to prevent bandits. I heard that the eastern part of Sichuan has also frequently reported unrest recently. When the reporter stayed overnight in Wanxian, I originally wanted to go ashore for a tour, but after learning that transportation was inconvenient after nine o'clock at night, and remote places had already declared martial law, I had to give up disappointedly. Having nothing to do on the boat, I leaned on the railing alone, looking at the lights of thousands of homes in the city, the night scene was magnificent, rarely seen elsewhere. At five o'clock in the afternoon on the 2nd of this month, the ship arrived in Chongqing and docked at the Jialing Wharf. The order was extremely chaotic. After landing, it was necessary to pass through an inspection station. On each street, pedestrians were like weaving, and vehicles were driving. Occasionally, there were those who did not obey traffic rules. The defects of Chongqing city lie in the lack of effort in order and cleanliness. After entering the city, I stayed at the YMCA and visited various places the next day to inquire about various situations. I learned that since the staff团 (military advisory group) entered Sichuan, the atmosphere in Chongqing has been renewed. Furthermore, Chairman Chiang Kai-shek personally came to supervise the suppression of bandits, encouraging the responsible leaders of Sichuan Province to be vigorous and self-reliant, to be loyal to their duties, and specifically proposed the five characters "公 (public)," "诚 (sincere)," "樸 (simple)," "拙 (honest)," "严 (strict)," ordering all levels of party, military, and government authorities in Sichuan Province, as well as all sectors of society, to abide by them, as the basis for revitalizing the spirit and changing the atmosphere. His prestige spread, and all the leaders of the Sichuan army obeyed orders respectfully, washing away the past decadent atmosphere. The reporter once talked with one or two people who have lived in Sichuan for a long time. They deeply lamented the various aspects of Sichuan in the past, with a feeling that there was a twenty-four history and not knowing where to begin. According to a certain gentleman from the academic circle who has lived in Sichuan for many years, in the past twenty-three years in Sichuan, there have been more than 470 large and small internal wars. The exorbitant taxes under the defense zone system are really unspeakable. For example, the military salaries and provisions in a certain military district were levied once a month. Various armies levied taxes under various names, and there were more than 700 customs checkpoints throughout the province. Some of the pre-collected money and grain had already reached the 69th year of the Republic of China. Several years ago, a certain army cleverly set up a name and levied a manure tax, arousing the public anger of the local people, who rose up in opposition. Although the result was not realized, it had already caused the people of Sichuan to lament, "Never in ancient times has manure been taxed, and now only farts are left without taxes." Also, a certain magistrate of Luxian County increased his income by specifically collecting lazy taxes from farmers who did not grow opium, from the countryside to the city, even from people without land who could grow opium. The people were resentful, so when he stepped down, they presented him with the couplet, "Leave one day earlier, Heaven has eyes, stay here for a long time, the earth has no skin," showing the tyranny of the government. After Chairman Chiang Kai-shek entered Sichuan, in addition to deploying the front-line bandit suppression military affairs, he also paid great attention to reforming Sichuan's politics. The 別動隊 (special action teams) led by the chairman's headquarters patrolled various places, observed the people's conditions, and many local tyrants and evil gentry were exposed. The most well-known special action team executed Shen Wenying, a major morphine manufacturer, in Chongqing, which was applauded by the people of Sichuan. Shen was a well-known Sichuan local leader who had run rampant in northern Sichuan for many years. In the past, he had been arrested by the Sichuan authorities several times, but was always released. This time, the special action team disguised themselves as detectives and learned all the details, destroyed his morphine manufacturing den, and executed him. Therefore, when the people of Chongqing talked about this matter, they mostly praised the efforts of the special action team. It is heard that many other bad elements have also been arrested one after another, and the trend of corruption has been slightly curbed. If it can be further thoroughly cleaned up, it will have a greater effect on reforming Sichuan's politics. The breaking of the defense zone system is also one of Chairman Chiang Kai-shek's political achievements after entering Sichuan. Sichuan had formed a strict defense zone system since the "Jingchuan Campaign" in the ninth year of the Republic of China. Not only could the central government not intervene, but even the military commander could not manage the division commander's defense zone, and the division commander could not restrain the brigade commander's defense zone. In this way, the entire province was divided into many small defense zones under the large defense zone. The soldiers controlled everything in their jurisdiction, colluding with local evil gentry, and levying exorbitant taxes. The people of Sichuan could not bear their suffering and fled their homes. Therefore, when Xu Xiangqian led several thousand hungry and exhausted people, he was able to run rampant in northern Sichuan for a time. The spread of banditry was mainly due to this reason. When people in Sichuan talked about bandits, they often said, "In the past, the bandits in Sichuan were welcomed in by the poor people of Sichuan." Although the words are plain, they contain profound meaning. Therefore, if the defense zone system is not broken, military affairs cannot be advanced, and politics cannot be reformed. Chairman Chiang Kai-shek's plan to reorganize Sichuan Province started with breaking the defense zone system. On the one hand, he carried out the reorganization and reduction of the Sichuan army, and on the other hand, he tried his best to break the decades-old idea of Sichuan people governing Sichuan. So far, the defense zone system can be said to have been completely broken. The Sichuan army is transferred, only listening to the orders of the central government. The reduction of the army has also been largely completed. The original Sichuan army had about 300 regiments, about 500,000 people. Now it has been reduced to 200 regiments, about 250,000 people. Military pay has been reduced to 40 million yuan, accounting for about two-thirds of the province's financial expenditure. Sichuan's politics has also made some progress compared to the past. According to those familiar with Sichuan's political situation, before the staff团 (military advisory group) entered Sichuan, most of the agencies below the provincial government did not work on time. Recently, they have strictly adhered to office hours, and most civil servants are energetic, willing to work hard and diligently. The recent change of the heads of the departments of civil affairs, construction, and education is deeply satisfying to the people of Sichuan, who believe that this is the initial step in reforming Sichuan's politics, enabling it to move towards construction.

Sichuan's finance has always been chaotic. Almost all banks issue banknotes, and the types of banknotes are also numerous, divided into savings certificates, exchange certificates, gift certificates, etc. The main business of the banks is not to engage in lending and savings, but to specialize in running remittance speculation, in order to make profits. Last year, Meifeng Bank made a profit of 600,000 yuan from running remittance, and used more than 300,000 yuan to build the Meifeng Building, a magnificent building, adding a lot of color to Chongqing's financial circles. However, on the other hand, many banks, such as commercial local banks, etc., suffered heavy losses due to the failure of running remittance. It is heard that the recently occurring issue of recalling local bank banknotes is actually related to the Xun remittance speculation issue. Because the reserve funds of local banks are only 6 million yuan, while the amount of banknotes issued is as high as 10 million yuan. In this case, it is naturally difficult to redeem them. In order to stabilize Sichuan's finance, the central government is doing its best to concentrate the right of issuance, and is recalling local banknotes at an 80% discount. Now the Central Bank has set up eleven exchange offices in various parts of Sichuan, limiting the people to exchange local banknotes for central banknotes at an 80% discount before November. However, most of these local banknotes are in the hands of the lower and middle classes of the southern border, and only this class suffers losses. If they are wealthy merchants, their deposits have already been deposited in banks, and they can not be affected.

With the deep-rooted problems of Sichuan Province, it is natural to have many difficulties in fundamentally reforming it in a short period of time. For example, in terms of finance, it still shows a situation of exhausting all resources. Monthly income and expenditure are insufficient by more than 2 million yuan. As of recently, the central bank has advanced funds amounting to 10 million yuan, borrowed 3 million yuan from the Central Bank, and borrowed 1 million yuan from the Farmers Bank. Therefore, the Sichuan Provincial Government has specially organized a financial reorganization committee, the purpose of which is to make finance public, reorganize finance, and reorganize provincial taxes. How will it be effective later? It remains to be seen. However, judging from the general situation, the future of Sichuan is generally optimistic. The people of Sichuan have been groaning for a long time, and they have great expectations for the central government. Every time the reporter talks with the people of Sichuan, between their words, they have enthusiastic expectations for the future of Sichuan, whether in military affairs, politics, industrial development, transportation construction, and education. Regarding education, such as Ren Hongjun's being the president of Sichuan University, and Hu Shuhua's being the president of Chongqing University, everyone is happy to have found the right person. Regarding transportation, the Sichuan-Guizhou Highway has been fully opened to traffic, and the Mianyang-Zitong section of the Sichuan-Shaanxi Highway has recently been completed. It is heard that the Chengdu-Chongqing Railway is also being planned and implemented. In the future, transportation will become more and more convenient, and industrial development will not be very difficult. Sichuan Province has very rich resources, with coal, iron, and oil production. The province has a population of 50 million and an area of more than 1.3 million square miles. The future development is limitless. The reporter has not been in Chongqing for long, but I feel that the morale of the people of Sichuan is more vigorous than that of the southeastern provinces. This is really a gratifying phenomenon.

Content of the Dalian Conference 68

With Tada's Proposition as the Main Topic: Resolved to Quickly Resolve the North China Issues

Beiping Correspondence: Japanese military officers recently held a meeting in Dalian. Before its opening, Okamura, who conveyed the Japanese government's intentions, made a speech, roughly saying that it was purely to convey the Japanese government's new policy towards China at the four-minister meeting. In the future, Japanese diplomats and army and navy officers stationed in China must handle all negotiations in accordance with the new policy, in order to be unified. The important Japanese figures attending the meeting also discussed what they should do. The main topic was based on the booklet "Basic Concepts on China" published by Tada Hayao, commander of the Japanese army stationed in Tianjin, on the Emperor's Birthday. As a result, the following three items seem to have been decided: (1) Japan is not prepared to build anything in North China at present, but economic cooperation, especially the development of North China's assets, should be carried out effectively in the short term. This matter will be handled by the South Manchuria Railway Company. (2) Anti-Japanese actions in Central and South China should be corrected by rapid methods, so as not to hinder Sino-Japanese friendship. (3) The outstanding issues in North China should be negotiated and resolved quickly, targeting the national government. (19th)

Henan, Hebei, Shandong, Jiangsu: Meeting on Closing Breaches and Restoring Dikes 69

Agreed on the Distribution of Construction Funds, and Requested Central Government Subsidies

Kaifeng Correspondence: The meeting of the four provinces of Henan, Hebei, Shandong, and Jiangsu on closing breaches and restoring dikes was held at the Yellow River Conservancy Commission at 4:00 p.m. on the 15th. The attendees were Kong Xiangrong and Zhang Hanying from the commission, Xu Xinwu, Wang Junyu, Liu Bingzhong representing the Henan Flood Control Supervisory Office, Zhang Honglie and Zhang Lianjia representing Shandong, Qi Shou'an representing Hebei, Yu Shufang representing Jiangsu, and Song Tong representing Henan. Those present included Zhou Li, Li Shilin, Zhu Xinlian, An Lisen, Gu Hongxi, Cai Zhen, Lu Keming, Liu Binghuang, Luo Zhongmao, and Gan Bochen. After Chairman Kong Xianrong opened the meeting, Mr. Kong gave a speech first, and then the representatives of the four provinces of Henan, Hebei, Shandong, and Jiangsu reported successively, followed by discussion of various proposals. (1) The Henan Provincial Government proposed the project of repairing the Yellow River dikes (total construction fund of 898,159 yuan). (2) The Hebei Provincial Government proposed the outline of the Yellow River dike restoration project in Hebei Province (total construction fund of 375,000 yuan). (3) The Shandong Provincial Government proposed that the funds required for the dike restoration project in Shandong are very large, and it is really difficult for this province to allocate funds. Please give priority to subsidies from the central government's dike restoration project funds (total construction fund of 11,273,560 yuan). (4) The Shandong Provincial Government proposed to allocate funds to repair the Zhukou dangerous project (including construction fund of 162,600 yuan). (5) The Shandong Provincial Government proposed to allocate funds to repair the dikes on both sides of the Yellow River (including construction fund of 1,674,000 yuan). (6) The Jiangsu Provincial Government proposed the summary of the post-disaster project plan for closing breaches and restoring dikes in the flooded area of northern Jiangsu (total construction fund of 3,930,200 yuan). (7) The Shandong Provincial Government representative temporarily proposed that the third item of the Dongzhuang breach closure project plan in Shandong Province, the Zhudi section dike project (80,494.52 yuan), the seventh item, the restoration of people's dikes (46,875 yuan), and the ninth item, the post-disaster project (388,600 yuan, etc.) Although related to closing breaches, they have the nature of dike restoration, and it is proposed to allocate funds from the dike restoration project to handle them (total construction fund of 415,969.52 yuan). The above seven proposals were discussed together, and it was resolved that the total construction fund listed in the above proposals was 18,722,988.92 yuan, and the central government's proposed subsidy was 1 million yuan, which was only 5% and was naturally insufficient. It was necessary to allocate subsidies according to the number of workers, scope, and importance of the projects listed by each province. The resolutions are as follows: (1) Of the projects proposed by Henan Province, the first is to restore the protective revetment of the Shu Batou, (item 6 in the original proposal's appendix), the second is to build the new dike on Yangzhuang Beach (item 7 in the original proposal's appendix), and the second is the Wenxian Gouzhaizhuang Shunshui dam project (item 9 in the original proposal's appendix), totaling 147,003 yuan. Please subsidize half of the amount from the central government, which is 73,500 yuan, and the rest should be raised locally to start construction. (2) Of the projects proposed by Hebei Province, the remedy for river course migration (item B in the original proposal) totals 100,000 yuan. Please subsidize half of the amount from the central government, which is 50,000 yuan, and the rest should be raised locally to start construction. (3) Of the projects proposed by Shandong Province, the first is the Zhudi section dike project (item 3 in the Dongzhuang breach closure plan appendix), the second is the restoration of people's dikes project (item 7 in the Dongzhuang breach closure plan appendix), the third is the post-disaster project (item 9 in the Dongzhuang breach closure plan appendix), and the fourth is the repair of the Zhukou dangerous project (proposal 4), the above four items total 581,969 yuan. Please subsidize half of the amount from the central government, which is 291,000 yuan, and the rest should be raised locally to start construction. This is related to the Yellow River itself. Furthermore, the Shandong Provincial Government proposed to repair the dikes of the Yunhe, Zhuhe, Wanfu and other rivers, and the banks of Zhaoyang, Nanyang, Weishan and other lakes (proposal 3), totaling more than 11.2 million yuan. This is a restoration project outside the scope of the Yellow River flood. Please have the central government use the remaining 241,800 yuan of the 1 million yuan for this allocation, and hand it over to the local government to consider the urgency and select the key points for construction within the breach closure and dike restoration project. The above subsidies for Shandong total 532,800 yuan. (4) The breach closure part of the project proposed by Jiangsu Province also belongs to the scope of the flood (item 1 in the original proposal), with a total estimate of 687,500 yuan. This breach closure part is the most important part of the dike restoration project. Please subsidize half of the amount from the central government, which is 343,700 yuan, and the local government should raise equal construction funds to start construction. (Note) The above-mentioned half of the subsidized construction funds are all rounded to the nearest hundred yuan for the convenience of calculation. (8) The representatives of each province temporarily proposed that the projects listed in this proposal are all important. In addition to the parts that have been decided to be subsidized by the central government and those that will be undertaken by the local government for half of the cost, the remaining construction funds are severely insufficient. It is proposed to submit the case to the central government for approval. Resolution: The original proposals will be forwarded to the National Economic Commission for approval. The meeting adjourned at 8:00 p.m. Zhang Lianjia left Bian early on the morning of the 16th to plan for the breach closure. Zhang Honglie and others also returned to Lu and Su on the night of the 16th and the 17th respectively to report. (17th)

Nanchang Chamber of Commerce Petitions for Emergency Curb on the Bankruptcy Trend 73

Please Handle Strictly by the Provincial Government to Maintain the Market and Avoid Panic

Nanchang Correspondence: The trend of bankruptcy in the markets of Jiangxi Province has been emerging frequently recently. The provincial and municipal chambers of commerce had previously petitioned the provincial government and the Department of Finance for relief due to the bankruptcy of Fukunheng, Zhang Zhengshun, Wu Peiji, and the Huyuansing Six-Union Company. Unexpectedly, Yilongxin recently went bankrupt, so the remitting and exchange guild and the money industry guild were deeply afraid that the bankruptcy trend would open up and become unmanageable. Therefore, they held a joint meeting yesterday and decided to ask the executive committee of the municipal chamber of commerce to petition the provincial government and the Department of Finance. For bankruptcy stores, administrative agencies should deal with them severely. The municipal chamber of commerce has submitted a report to the provincial government, conveying the situation. The report stated, "According to a letter from the Nanchang remitting and exchange guild and the Nanchang money industry guild, we have seen that the bankruptcy trend has been very strong recently, and the market is shaking. In general, shops and households are afraid of making loans and deposits. At this time of financial exhaustion and tight credit, it is unfortunate that bankruptcy events have occurred one after another, such as Fukunheng, Zhang Zhengshun, Wupeiji Zhuang, Huyuanxing, and six households, which have been suspended for less than ten days. Debts are piling up, affecting the entire market. Now the bankruptcy of Yilongxin is also reported. If a method is not established to prohibit it, I am afraid that the bankruptcy trend will repeatedly occur and follow, and I do not know where it will end. It is investigated that bankruptcy cases have always been prosecuted in court, and often involve legal language, wasting time and delaying matters. By the time of execution, it is unknown how long it will take to conclude. The result is nothing more than bankruptcy. Those cunning debtors will also hide their property in advance and secretly hoard it. After the case is closed, they are still rich family members, while the creditors have suffered heavy losses. This is especially painful. If the law is not respected, people will not know the punishment. If the prevention is not strict, the malpractice cannot be stopped. Our associations have jointly discussed, all in order to maintain the market and curb the bankruptcy trend. For bankruptcy cases, the administrative agency should formulate a temporary regulation for severe measures. In the event of a bankruptcy case, creditors can apply to the administrative agency for strict handling, so as to avoid delaying time, and the debtors can be free from the law. If this is done with lightning speed, the bankruptcy trend can be reduced, and the market will not be greatly panicked. In addition to submitting to the Provincial Government Department of Finance, a corresponding letter is sent to your association, please investigate and hope to transfer it for review and implementation. Based on this, it is found that the market bankruptcy trend is emerging frequently, and if it is not quickly prohibited, it is not enough to maintain the market and reassure the people. The methods described in the letter from the guild, etc., are for temporary relief and cannot be said to be unreasonable. However, it is not easy to draft the regulations, and we should ask your government to first issue an emergency announcement to sternly warn the people. If there are bankruptcy incidents, we will first instruct the Public Security Bureau and the county government to strictly investigate and deal with them to supplement the judicial office's inadequacies. Hopefully, the bankruptcy trend can be stopped, and the market can be free from panic. There is no better way to save the day than this." (October 18)

Zhang and Su's Factions Already Defeated; Huang's Bandit Gang Also Scattered

Fuzhou Correspondence: Jiang Dingwen, the Pacification Commissioner of Fujian, arrived in the province on the 12th from Zhangzhou. As for the recent bandit suppression situation on the Fujian-Zhejiang border, there was a communist bandit faction in southern Zhejiang led by Zhang Yunlong, Su Yu (also known as Liu Hannan), and Huang Fuwu. According to a report from Shi Er, the magistrate of Fuan County, stationed in eastern Fujian, the first regiment of his unit is engaged in fierce fighting with Xie Zuolin's faction at the junction of Xiapu and Fuding, and the third regiment is engaged in fierce fighting with Fan Tiemin's faction at the junction of Shouning and Fuan. The security regiments are also mobilized to assist in the suppression, and the situation is expected to be resolved within a few days. Furthermore, according to a telegram from Commander Liu of Jian'ou County, stationed in northern Fujian, after Huang Ligui's faction fled into the border area between Jian'ou and Jianyang, Commander Liu immediately夹击the bandits with the troops of Commander Zhou Zhiqun's division. The bandits initially resisted stubbornly in the dangerous passes of Dongshan Cenyang and other areas, and then scattered into the mountains. Troops are being dispatched to search for them. Additionally, the Big Sword Society bandits in Yanping and Shaxian counties have all surrendered, handing over their talismans, swords, guns, and banners. Dai Minquan, the garrison division commander, and Tang Yintang, the commissioner, specially led troops to the bandit areas to appease and encourage them to start anew, in order to stabilize the situation. Local News

International Trade Bureau Releases This Year's Foreign Trade Situation: Trade Volume for the First Half of the Year Totals Over 800 Million Yuan; a Decrease of Approximately 4 Percent Compared to the Same Period in Previous Years 83

According to the New New News Agency, He Bingxian, Director of the International Trade Bureau, announced that foreign trade this year continues to decline, but without a significant decrease. In terms of the total trade volume, the first quarter amounted to 389,818,892 yuan. The third quarter saw a slight increase, amounting to 415,006,077 yuan. The total for the first half of the year was 808,824,968 yuan, a decrease of 4 percent compared to the same period in previous years. The details are as follows:

Trade Situation in the First Six Months: Compared to the same period last year, foreign trade in the first six months of this year showed a better export performance in the first quarter, with each month exceeding the same period last year by 8 or 9 percent. February was equivalent to 97.34 percent. The second quarter saw a decline. Except for April, which exceeded the same month last year very slightly, May and June were only equivalent to 82-83 percent of the same month last year. On the import side, the situation was the opposite of exports. Each month in the first quarter was lower than the same month in previous years, while each month in the second quarter exceeded the same month in previous years. The highest, such as June, even exceeded by 6.11 percent, mainly due to the sharp increase in grain imports this year. In terms of the total amount, except for April, each month was lower than the same period last year. Regarding the issue of gold and silver imports and exports, which is related to the trade balance, in the first half of this year, due to the implementation of various government restrictions on silver exports and the inflow of foreign capital, silver exports not only decreased sharply by 92 percent compared to the same period last year, but silver imports also increased by 2.7 million yuan compared to the previous year. As for raw gold and gold coins, the import value was over 112,000 gold units, and the export value was over 13.969 million gold units, which also decreased compared to the same period last year.

Trade Values and Gold Conversion Changes: However, when observing the figures in gold conversion, the situation is quite different. Regardless of imports or exports, they are mostly higher than the same period last year. The US dollar value of exports was still the highest in January, at over 19.07 million gold dollars. February and March were the lowest, but still reached over 14 million gold dollars. Compared to the gold conversion value of exports in the same period last year, all months showed an increase. The US dollar value of imports was the highest in April and May, each amounting to over 39 million gold dollars. February was the lowest, but still reached over 24.09 million gold dollars. Compared to the same period last year, except for January and February, which decreased by 15 percent, the remaining months all showed an increase. June even increased by more than 30 percent. As for the total amount, the situation was roughly the same. The reason why the gold conversion figures this year exceeded the same period last year is mainly due to the rise in silver prices. The highest gold conversion rate for the national currency in the same period last year was 0.34290. This year, the silver price涨风was strong, and the exchange rate of the national currency against the US dollar increased from 24 cents in January to 40 cents in June. Therefore, in the first half of this year, the value of China's foreign trade, when calculated in银方商, showed a lower degree of export decline than import decline. Exports decreased by 2 percent, and imports decreased by 4 percent. However, when calculated in gold conversion, the degree of import increase was equal to exports, with exports increasing by 10 percent and imports increasing by 9.5 percent. The close relationship between the changes in silver prices and trade values can be seen from this.

Import Surplus Values in the First Half of This Year: The import surplus in the first half of this year totaled 286,085,622 yuan, a decrease of over 15,219,000 yuan compared to the same period last year. The reason why the import surplus figure was lower in the first half of this year was due to the decline in import trade in the first quarter of this year. The total import surplus in the first quarter of this year was over 118 million yuan, a decrease of no less than 40 million yuan compared to the same period last year. However, in the second quarter, due to the sharp increase in rice imports, the import surplus reached over 167 million yuan, an increase of over 25 million yuan compared to the same period last year. Otherwise, the import surplus in the first half of this year would have been even lower. If we observe the percentage of the import surplus in the total import amount for each month, the foreign trade balance in the first half of this year was not better than the same period last year. In the same period last year, the average monthly import surplus accounted for 52.87 percent of the total import amount. This year, it also accounted for 52.45 percent. The highest, such as March and April, even accounted for over 59.87 percent, which was unseen in the same period last year. Fortunately, exports were strong in January and February, so the import surplus only accounted for 37-38 percent of the total population value of that month. Otherwise, the percentage of the import surplus in the total population amount in the first half of this year would have been close to the peak of the first half of 1933 (61 percent).

Promoting Acceptance Bill Measures 94

Xinxin News Agency reports: The Shanghai Industrial and Commercial Loan Review Committee, in order to support industrial and commercial sectors, encourage production, and circulate domestic goods, has allocated two million yuan as a fund for auctioning acceptance bills. The draft has been completed and will be submitted to the committee for approval today, and then submitted to the Ministry for approval before implementation. The draft measures are excerpted as follows: (1) In order to support industrial and commercial sectors, encourage production, circulate domestic goods, and maintain the livelihood of workers, this committee, with the consent of various participating banks and money houses, and with the approval of the Ministry of Finance, will allocate three million yuan of national currency from the small credit loan to be used as a fund for industrial and commercial bill acceptance or guarantee and discounting, and the national treasury voucher issued by the Ministry will still be used as the second guarantee. (2) This bill acceptance or guarantee shall be entrusted to be handled by this committee after consulting with various banks and money houses. All handling fees shall be borne by the applicant. (3) The above bill acceptance or guarantee shall be submitted to this committee for review by the entrusted institution. According to the amount, the national treasury voucher will be issued as proof of the second guarantee. (4) The method of acceptance or guarantee is as follows: A. If industrial and commercial sectors store raw materials and goods in warehouses, and after appraisal, they are in demand in the market and have value, and have undergone transfer procedures, they may fill out bank acceptance bills according to the discount stipulated in these measures, and the entrusted institution will accept them. B. The face value of the bill requested for acceptance by industrial and commercial sectors shall not exceed 60% of the estimated value of the goods provided as collateral. The acceptance period shall not exceed four months. C. If the holder of the aforementioned acceptance bill needs it, he may apply for discounting to the entrusted discounting institution. The discounting rate is 8% per month. The institution handling the discounting shall report the name and amount of the discounter to the committee daily. (5) When the bank acceptance bill expires, the applicant shall pay the amount to the entrusted institution as scheduled. If it is not paid as scheduled, in addition to filling in the payment, the entrusted institution may sell the raw materials and goods provided as collateral for compensation. If there is any shortfall, it may also recover from the original bill stakeholders. (6) When the commercial acceptance bill expires, the acceptor shall pay the amount as scheduled. If it is not paid as scheduled, in addition to filling in the payment, the entrusted institution may recover from the bill stakeholders. (7) The amount of bill acceptance or guarantee is temporarily limited to three million yuan. If the applicant has paid it upon expiration, the committee may continue to handle the acceptance or guarantee within its quota. (8) In addition to the above regulations, all rules issued by the Ministry of Finance to this committee shall apply. (9) These measures shall be implemented from the date of approval by the Ministry of Finance.
