The Chinese Industrial Chemical Research Institute Successfully Researches Spray Paint; Another Great Contribution in the Tide of Advocating Domestic Goods 98

The Chinese Industrial Chemical Research Institute on Pobo Road in this city has been established for six years. It is dedicated to developing domestic production and promoting new industries as its basic research purpose. Over the years, it has made many creations to the chemical industry. Recently, the preliminary test of lacquer has been completed. According to Dr. Pan Lujie, director of the institute, lacquer is an excellent product for decorating and protecting wooden and ironware, commonly known as spray paint. It is used on cars, high-end ironware, and woodenware. Its texture is strong, it dries quickly, it is very heat-resistant, and its luster is beautiful, which is incomparable to other paints or varnishes. Therefore, the number of Chinese people who love to use lacquer is increasing. It is heard that all the woodenware in the International Hotel in Shanghai uses lacquer instead of paint, which shows that the advantages of lacquer have been recognized by most people. However, it is a pity that this lacquer is all imported, and the outflow of rights and interests every year is very large. Although there has been a small amount of domestic lacquer in recent years, its basic raw materials still come from foreign countries, and most of the benefits ultimately go to the coffers of other countries. This time, the Chinese Industrial Chemical Research Institute used domestic cotton as a starting point, and after considerable treatment, made nitrocellulose. The nitric acid and other auxiliary drugs used in it are also all pure domestic products. The quality of the nitrocellulose obtained is not inferior to the best European and American goods, so-called "quarter-second nitrocellulose" (according to the inspection of nitrocellulose, it is best to drop a steel ball into the solution of nitrocellulose, and it is best to drop ten inches in a quarter of a second, followed by dropping ten inches in half a second, and so on). In addition, various synthetic gums used in lacquer are also in the program of the research institute. The so-called "organic salt glue" has also achieved satisfactory results. Its crystals are transparent and do not stain. It is most suitable for lacquer with bright colors. The "organic salt glue" is also made entirely from domestic raw materials. This research has been carried out for more than a year, and the staff has often forgotten to eat and sleep and worked day and night without the slightest slack. Their hope for the successful development of industry is like this. The Chinese Industrial Chemical Research Institute is an academic research institution founded by Mr. Wu Yun Chu and Tianchu MSG Factory. It is committed to public service. Whether it is a factory or an individual, it can take advantage of its exquisite equipment and extensive experience, and its complete library is an indispensable resource for chemical technology.

Technician Yao Shiyan of the Chinese Industrial Chemical Research Institute is photographed while testing the viscosity of nitrocellulose.

Ministry of Finance Instructs the Niter and Sulfur Bureau to Promote Domestic Niter, Sulfur, and Sulfuric Acid 100

Various Industries Must Try Their Best to Use Domestic Products; Kaicheng Acid Manufacturing Company Has Abundant Production

The Ministry of Finance instructed the Jiangsu Niter and Sulfur Bureau to promote domestic niter, sulfur, and sulfuric acid. The order said: Since the Ministry took over the niter and sulfur affairs, it has made unremitting efforts to revitalize domestic niter and sulfur products. For the niter part, the Kaiyue Niter Refining Factory has been purchasing raw niter to refine fine niter. This fine niter contains potassium nitrate, which is more than 99% of the ingredients, which is no less than imported products. Relying on supplying the needs of the whole country, the effect is gradually obvious. Recently, the Ministry will collect niter from various domestic niter-producing areas, such as Xuhai in Jiangsu, Caodan in Shandong, 21 counties in northern Anhui, and the entire province of Hebei, and hand over the niter collection affairs to the factory for processing, in order to increase raw materials and expand sales. For the sulfur part, the three provinces of Hunan, Hubei, and Henan have the most abundant output. The Ministry has repeatedly ordered to improve quality and reduce costs, and ordered various provinces to use them as much as possible. Recently, an improved sulfur refining test farm was established in Xinan, Henan Province, using the latest scientific methods to actively improve manufacturing to facilitate sales. In addition, potassium chlorate has always been supplied by foreign countries, and no factory in China has set up its own factory to manufacture it. The Salt Administration of the Ministry has repeatedly established a potassium chlorate manufacturing research committee to study all matters related to the establishment and manufacture of potassium chlorate, and hired experienced industrialists in China to jointly study to ensure progress on record. All these efforts to revitalize domestic products are to stop loopholes and assist industry and commerce, and are also beneficial to the overall management of niter and sulfur and the increase of tax revenue. It is now found that sulfuric acid is also a kind of niter and sulfur products, and the number of domestic users is very large. In the past, because our country produced rare, mostly purchased from imports, the outflow of rights and interests is countless. Recently, domestic acid manufacturing plants, such as Shanghai Kaicheng Acid Manufacturing Company and Tianjin Lizhong Acid Manufacturing Factory, manufacture sulfuric acid with abundant production. For the sake of revitalizing the country, it should be promoted. It is hereby ordered that the bureau should immediately follow the instructions, and transfer the order to the factories and users in the province. In the future, when purchasing and transporting sulfuric acid, they must try their best to use domestic products. As for how to strictly audit the uses of sulfuric acid in various industries to emphasize management, and how to effectively promote the sales of domestic sulfuric acid to cultivate tax sources, you should also refer to the situation in the province, and prepare detailed measures and submit them for review and handling. This order.

(C) Lecture Topics on Industrial and Commercial Accounting Class: (1) Accounting Essentials, (2) Accounting Subjects, (3) Preparation and Content of Financial Statements, (4) Outline of Asset Valuation, (5) Liabilities and Capital, (6) Calculation of Donations and Benefits, (7) Analysis and Explanation of Financial Statements, (8) Outline of Cost Accounting, (9) Outline of Bank Accounting, (10) Outline of Auditing. However, outsiders do not understand and think it is a private group, hoping to obtain some benefits after joining this association. It is a misunderstanding. This association is currently in the preparation period, which is expected to be completed by the end of the year, and it will be officially established in January next year.

Public Concession Population Census Scheduled for the 23rd, Verifying the Actual Number of Chinese and Foreign Residents within the Concession, Distributing Census Forms for Advance Completion 108

The population census within the Public Concession, conducted every five years by the Municipal Council, is scheduled for the evening of the 23rd of this month. The purpose is to verify the actual increase or decrease in the number of Chinese and foreign residents within the concession over the past five years. The notice from the Municipal Council is transcribed below:

"Notice is hereby given that the Shanghai Public Concession conducts a population census of residents, Chinese and foreign, every five years. The last census was conducted in the 19th year of the Republic of China (1930). This year marks the time for another census. The purpose of the census is to ascertain any changes in the residents within the concession since the last census. The date for the census has been set for the evening of October 23rd of this year. Prior to this, on the 22nd or 23rd during the day, census takers dispatched by the Municipal Council will distribute blank census forms to each household within the concession. Each household should fill in the form with the number of family members residing in the household on that day (October 23rd), the number of people, as well as their gender, age, occupation, etc. It should be noted that this census is solely for population statistics and will not be used for any other purpose. It is hoped that each head of household will fill in the form in detail according to the items listed, and keep it for the census taker to retrieve. If there is anything unclear, please consult with relatives and neighbors for clarification. Otherwise, when the census taker comes to collect the form, please ask for their assistance in filling it out.

Shanghai Public Concession Municipal Council"

China Merchants Steam Navigation Company and Nine Other Companies to Collect Cash for Water Freight on Yichang-Chongqing Route, Notice Effective Today 110

Nine shipping companies operating on the Shanghai-Yichang-Chongqing route, including the state-owned China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, the private Sanbei, Ningshao, and Minsheng companies, the British Taikoo and Jardine Matheson companies, the Japanese Nissin company, the Italian Italian-Chinese Navigation Company, and the French Compagnie Maritime et Fluviale de l'Indochine, have decided in a joint meeting that all cargo water freight will be collected in cash from today onwards. The notice is transcribed below:

"We hereby announce that the industry association has jointly decided that, starting from October 21st (Monday), all cargo shipped from Shanghai to Yichang and Chongqing, regardless of whether it is transshipped or direct, will have all water freight collected in cash. Payment can be made at the port of departure (Shanghai) to receive the bill of lading, or payment can be made at the port of arrival (Yichang or Chongqing) to pick up the goods. However, water freight paid at the port of arrival will only be accepted in Central Bank banknotes. In addition to sending letters to each customer and customs broker, this notice is hereby given for your information."

Japanese Theater "Kabuki-za" Experienced a False Alarm the Night Before Last, Violent Explosion at the Feet of a Japanese Soldier, Entire Venue in Chaos, Fortunately No Injuries 111

According to the Shanghai Nichinichi Shimbun, at 7 PM on the 19th, while the Japanese theater "Kabuki-za" on North Sichuan Road was showing the famous film "Railway," a violent explosion occurred suddenly at the feet of Yamamoto Sotaro, a third-class seaman from the warship Iwate, who was seated in the front row on the left side near the stage. Sparks flew everywhere. All the spectators in the venue, upon seeing this, were shocked and lost their color, and rushed to escape. The venue was in chaos for a time. Upon hearing the news, the Japanese Consulate Police Station immediately dispatched a large number of police chiefs and detectives, together with officers from the Dixwell Road Police Station, to rush to the theater to investigate. Fortunately, there were no injuries. However, a corner of the sailor's trousers was scorched by the fire. Furthermore, it was found that the explosive device was made by filling gunpowder into a glass bottle, with brown liquid left on the ground. It appeared to have been made with highly flammable materials such as sulfuric acid and gunpowder. However, there was no fuse. It was probably placed there beforehand, and exploded after a certain period of time.

Lu Zhulin, Wang Zhihao, and other detectives from the French Police recently cracked a case involving Xu Decai, alias Xu Datou, a well-known pickpocket king in this port, and four accomplices, Wang Dehua, Yuan Hailin, and Hu Asheng, and transferred them to the Special Second Court for interrogation and detention. This was reported in the previous newspaper. After the case occurred, detectives Guo Shaorong and others continued to apprehend six pickpocket accomplices, Yuan Liansheng (20 years old, from Nanjing), Wu Shaoshan (23 years old, from Shanghai), Lu Jinsheng (24 years old, from Jiading), Li Amao (21 years old, from Jiangbei), Li Hailou (28 years old, from Tianjin), and Ji Jinsheng (also known as Amao, 24 years old, from Suzhou). These individuals specialized in using crowded gatherings outside streetcars, movie theaters, and shops as opportunities to practice their skills of stealthily pilfering. They were all led by the previously arrested Xu Datou. It is rumored that some police officers receive salaries from these individuals, which is why it is difficult to crack cases and bring them to justice. This time, the net of justice is vast and spares nothing, and they were caught off guard, which can be said to be the end of their days. The police transferred the above six defendants to the Special Second Court, where Judge Zhang Chaozuo conducted a preliminary hearing. Because the police investigation was not yet complete, a request for postponement was made. The court ordered that the hearing be rescheduled for the 25th, and the defendants were remanded in custody. With this large-scale arrest and punishment of pickpockets by the French police, it is expected that the trend of pickpocketing in the French Concession will subside and be quiet for a while.

Jiang Xuesen, from Zhenjiang, over forty years old, runs Taixing Cigarette and Paper Store at No. 101, MacGaoPaul Road, French Concession. The police lawyer requested a postponement of the investigation to apprehend the accomplices at large and then request a trial. The court verified the report, questioned the defendant, and then approved the postponement for further investigation before another hearing. The defendant was remanded in custody.

Comprador's Outrageous Behavior, Impersonating a Public Official, Luring and Raping a Woman 114

Tang Qirong, a 24-year-old native of Zhenjiang working as a comprador, residing at No. 107, Huanlong Road, French Concession, is known for his outrageous behavior. On the night of the 11th of this month, at 11 PM, he encountered Huang Yumei, a 20-year-old woman from Yangzhou (currently residing at No. 17, Maisai Erdi Luo Road), who used to be a prostitute selling salt water but has now reformed. Tang immediately stopped Huang, impersonating a police detective and demanding to see her prostitute's license. Huang replied that she had already stopped her prostitution business and was no longer a prostitute. Upon hearing this, Tang still falsely claimed that he wanted to take Huang to a certain place for further investigation. In the darkness, he took the woman to a bedroom, forcibly raped her, and stayed overnight. The next morning, Tang promised to give the woman six yuan, instructing her to follow him to a certain place to collect the money. At the time, the woman was unable to resist due to her weakness and let him do as he pleased. The next morning, hearing Tang's promise of money, she did not hold a grudge and believed him to be true, and followed him out to collect the money. It turned out that Tang was a cunning man, and he designed an escape midway. The woman was unable to pursue him, cried in vain, and returned home disgruntled. The day before, Huang Yumei happened to meet Tang on the road and demanded the promised money. To her surprise, Tang not only ignored her, but also punched her, causing her injury. Subsequently, the woman found out Tang's address and reported it to the French Police. Detectives Zhang Zhaolin and Cao Chuanbiao arrested Tang. After an investigation, the next day, he was transferred to the First Criminal Division of the Special Second Court. The police lawyer explained the case, accusing the defendant of impersonating a public official, intimidating and defrauding, disrupting public morals, and causing injury, and filed a public prosecution. Subsequently, the plaintiff Huang Yumei stated the details of how the defendant falsely claimed to be a detective to inspect her license, lured her into rape, and caused injury. When questioned, the defendant's confession was evasive and cunning. After Judge Li Changnian verified the confession, he declared the facts clear, announced the end of the debate, and awaited a scheduled pronouncement of the verdict. The defendant was remanded in custody.

Municipal Zoo Purchases Large Turtle and Rare Tortoise, Large Turtle Weighs 30 Jin and is Already on Display, Rare Tortoise is Difficult to Exhibit Due to Cold Weather, Zheng Xiaoqiu Donates Beloved Goldfish 115

The Municipal Zoo on Wenmiao Road has recently added three new aquatic animals, all of which are valuable and have been put on display. A reporter from Datong News Agency investigated and reported the situation as follows:

Large Turtle: The zoo recently purchased a large turtle from a Cantonese man. It weighs 30 jin net, with a shell length of 22 inches and a width of 17 inches. When the head and tail are extended, the length reaches more than one foot. It is now kept in the same place as the fish in the aquatic category, which has aroused the interest of visitors.

Rare Tortoise: The zoo also purchased a rare tortoise. Although the shell is no different from ordinary tortoises, its tail has extremely obvious scales, and its head is in a special state. The mouth is sharp and resembles an eagle's beak. It can prey on fish and shellfish, and neither the head nor the tail can retract inwards. It is indeed rare, so it is specially named the "Eagle Scale Tortoise." Due to the increasingly cold weather, the tortoise urgently needs to hibernate in the mud layer, so the exhibition will have to wait.

Goldfish: Furthermore, Zheng Xiaoqiu, the director and actor of the Star Film Company, after the death of his father Zheng Zhengqiu, will move to live in the company. He intends to part with dozens of goldfish that he has raised for many years and donate them to the zoo. He has already sent someone to contact the zoo, and they will be sent to the zoo for display within the next few days, for people to enjoy.

Sixty-Odd Businesses Submit Petition to French Consul General, Requesting Reinstatement of Vegetable Stalls on Rue Conty 116

The vegetable stalls along Rue Conty in the French Concession have been ordered to be shut down by the French Police for more than a month, and the matter has not been resolved. The stall vendors have been running around appealing and petitioning the Chinese Taxpayers' Association and others, requesting assistance for relief. Details have been reported in this newspaper many times. It is now reported that over sixty businesses on Rue Conty, including Jiuda Xin, Fuyuan Sauce Garden, Xinchangsheng, Li Runde, Shentaichang, and Hengchang Yiji, have a close relationship with the vegetable stalls, and have jointly submitted a petition to the French Consul General Baudens, requesting that the Municipal Council be ordered to allow the establishment of vegetable stalls at the east end of Rue Conty to maintain the market. The original petition is as follows:

"Petition for Request: We, the undersigned, hereby submit this petition. The vegetable stalls on Rue Conty have been closed down by the French Police for more than a month, and have not been reinstated. As a result, the livelihoods of the vegetable vendors are in a state of panic. Some are starving to death, some are deeply in debt, and some have exhausted their possessions. The situation is dire, beyond words. We, the undersigned, are all businesses operating on Rue Conty and have witnessed the situation closely. We believe that if the matter is not resolved, the danger to their lives will only increase. The vegetable stalls have been established on Rue Conty since 1929 and have been operating for seven years. In June 1931, they were once closed down. We, the undersigned, jointly sent a letter to the French Consul General Fevrier, requesting permission to establish the stalls, and the request was approved. Since the establishment of the vegetable stalls on Rue Conty, the market has prospered and the businesses of the shops have been able to develop. The police's closure this time was caused by the relocation due to road repairs. In fact, it has nothing to do with traffic. At a time when commerce is extremely depressed and the people's livelihood is difficult to the extreme, the revitalization of the market is of utmost importance. We, the undersigned, feel that our relationship with the vegetable vendors is interdependent and cannot stand idly by. We hereby jointly petition Your Excellency the Consul General to safeguard commerce and order the Municipal Council to allow the establishment of vegetable stalls on the east end of Rue Conty to the end of Rue Louvain, to maintain the commercial market. This is for the public good. We humbly submit this petition to His Excellency Baudens, Consul General of the French Republic in Shanghai."

After Effective Production-Sales Cooperation, Match Industry Develops Relief Plan, Expanding Overseas Sales, Balancing Production and Sales, Small Factories Merge for Operation and Improve Products 117

According to the Industrial and Commercial News Agency, since the implementation of the production-sales cooperation policy in the domestic match industry, the industry has gradually recovered in just three months. A reporter interviewed a prominent merchant in the industry, who provided detailed information about the future development and relief plan. This is divided and recorded below:

Restricting Factory Establishment, Expanding Markets: Foreign merchants establish factories in China based on the commercial treaties signed in the past. The factory sites are mostly located in concessions where Chinese government orders do not apply. They also employ Chinese workers at low wages and use cheap Chinese raw materials to sell locally. Therefore, the domestic match industry is subject to the exploitation of foreign merchants. To protect the industry, China should promulgate measures to restrict the establishment of factories by foreign merchants. They must be registered and strictly examined before being allowed to establish factories to limit them. According to experts' estimates, domestic matches can produce 1 million cases annually, but domestic consumption is less than 700,000 cases. Therefore, in order to achieve a balance between production and sales, it is necessary to expand sales channels and develop overseas markets.

Reducing Import Taxes: China is already able to supply most of the raw materials for matches. However, several types of raw materials, such as red phosphorus, green barium sulfide, and paraffin oil, still need to be imported. The government should carefully examine the situation and reduce tax rates, and eliminate handling fees, so that Chinese merchants can reduce costs and expand sales channels. In addition, foreign matches sold at prices lower than cost should be subject to dumping duties.

Improving Quality, Merging Small Factories: Improving the quality of matches is the most important task at hand. In the past, Chinese matches were once sold in the Philippines and Manila, but they were stopped because (a) the matches were difficult to strike, and (b) the matchboxes were easily blocked. These are the points that need to be improved urgently. Since the implementation of production-sales cooperation, business has not been as bleak as in the past. However, domestic capital is weak and should be merged for operation to achieve large-scale production.

Two Rice Stores on Guangfu Road, Zhabei, Fined for Underreporting Quarterly Donations, Landlord Also Liable 118

The two rice stores, Jingcheng Rice Store at No. 297 and 299 Guangfu Road, Zhabei, and Qingda Rice Store at No. 293 next door, were found to have underreported their quarterly donations by Liu Wenzhan and Huang Xiting, investigators from the Municipal Finance Bureau's North District Tax Collection Office. The report was submitted to the office, which was forwarded to the Public Security Bureau, ordering Liao Jiongran, director of the Xinzha Branch, to investigate and punish them. After receiving the order, Director Liao immediately issued it to officer Huang Chongren, who dispatched police to summon Wang Changsheng, a partner of Jingcheng, 28 years old, and Hua Zhongjie, an accountant of Qingda, also 28 years old. Both partners were local residents. They both stated that the rent was set by the landlord Zhou Ziqi and denied underreporting the quarterly donations. Later, the monthly rent payment records were extracted and found to be inconsistent with the figures on the rent receipts. Jingcheng's actual monthly rent was 84 yuan, while the rent receipt only showed 48 yuan, underreporting 36 yuan per month. Qingda's actual monthly rent was 132 yuan, while the rent receipt also only showed 48 yuan, underreporting 84 yuan per month. Police were dispatched to

Summon the landlord Zhou Ziqi on Gonghe New Road and Heding Road, and rental contracts were retrieved to prove that the landlord and tenants colluded to underreport. After verification by Officer Huang, it was found that Jingcheng had underreported a rent of 36 yuan per month from March to the end of September this year, totaling seven months, amounting to 252 yuan. At 14%, the quarterly donation payable was 17 yuan, 6 jiao, 4 fen. A fine of 20% was imposed, amounting to 13 yuan, 5 jiao, 2 fen, 8 li, for a total of 21 yuan, 1 jiao, 6 fen, 8 li. Qingda, on the other hand, had underreported a rent of 84 yuan per month, also for seven months, amounting to 588 yuan. The quarterly donation payable was 41 yuan, 1 jiao, 6 fen, and the fine was 8 yuan, 2 jiao, 3 fen, 2 li, for a total of 49 yuan, 3 jiao, 9 fen, 2 li. In addition, Jingcheng owed 21 yuan, 1 jiao, 6 fen for the autumn quarter donation, and Qingda owed a total of 64 yuan, 8 jiao for the spring, summer, and autumn quarter donations, which were combined for collection.

Notice from the Tobacco Exchange Industry, Winter Licenses Allowed to Not Affix Stamps 119

The Shanghai Tobacco Exchange Industry Association's Shanghai office issued a notice to all members yesterday, stating:

"Notice is hereby given that the winter tobacco and alcohol licenses applied for by the members have been issued and dispatched to be distributed separately. All tax authorities have ordered the filling out of business status forms, ordering them to be filled out and reported quarterly, which is complicated. The association was requested to handle this on their behalf. This association has submitted a separate report to the Ministry of Finance and the collection agency, explaining the difficulties in handling it and requesting that it be handled according to the case. This has been approved. As for the license, as a rule, a one-fen stamp is affixed for each yuan. If there are omissions or errors in the posting, a heavy penalty will be imposed. Now, the new stamp tax law has been promulgated, and there is a misunderstanding that each license must be affixed with a one-yuan stamp. The members, in times of economic recession, are unable to bear the burden and requested the association to argue on reasonable grounds. This association has repeatedly sent letters to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce requesting the Ministry of Finance to amend and abolish it. This has been approved, and starting from the winter season, licenses are allowed to not affix stamps. This notice is hereby given for your information."

Municipal Public Security Bureau Handles Fire Insurance Policyholder Registration, To Crack Down on Small Assets Being Overinsured for Large Amounts 120

The Municipal Public Security Bureau believes that it is legitimate for the various residences, shops, factories, and warehouses in the city to take out fire insurance with various insurance companies for the safety of their property and to prevent unforeseen circumstances. However, the city is vast and has a diverse population, with good and bad mixed together. There are often unscrupulous people who insure small assets for large amounts, commit arson for compensation. Not only are the insurance companies deceived, but nearby residents are also harmed. To prevent this, the bureau has ordered all policyholders to register with the bureau to eliminate loopholes.

Amidst the Closing of the National Games, Public Buses Collide Twice, City-Run and Private Chinese Buses Seek Progress, Driver's Tickets Seriously Injured, Eight People, Some Critically Ill 124

According to the Central News Agency, the large number of spectators at the opening of the National Games made traffic management difficult, which was generally anticipated. Despite the painstaking coordination by Zhang Dengyi, head of the Traffic Division of the Games, the congestion of vehicles and the difficulty of directing them, such as the taxi parking lot being far from the main entrance of the Games, and the overloading of various public buses in order to solicit business, resulting in overturning and injuries, were all met with dissatisfaction by the general public. Unexpectedly, on the last day of the Games, a bloody tragedy occurred between drivers of Zhabei public buses and city-run public buses due to soliciting passengers, which was particularly unfortunate. The detailed situation is recorded as follows:

Cause of the Tragedy: After the opening of the Games, the Traffic Committee resolved to dispatch 30 city-run public buses to maintain traffic at the Games, and designated Beisichuan Road and Qiujiang Road as the passenger station for city-run public buses, and Baoshan Road and Qiujiang Road as the passenger station for private Chinese public buses, in order to avoid disputes between the two sides over soliciting passengers. Unexpectedly, after the opening of the Games, there were fewer passengers on Beisichuan Road and Qiujiang Road, and the city-run public buses moved to the same address on Baoshan Road, where there were more passengers, so there were disputes over soliciting passengers. This is one of the causes of the tragedy. The city-run public buses have larger bodies and more comfortable seats, and are city-run, so the general drivers tend to ignore the speed limit, and also like to chase other vehicles in the middle of the road to win the favor of passengers, so other vehicles feel jealous. This is the second reason that led to the fight between the drivers of both sides.

Process of the Tragedy: At 10:30 am yesterday, driver No. 314 of the city-run public bus had a dispute with the driver of the private Chinese bus at the intersection of Baoshan Road and Qiujiang Road due to soliciting passengers. At that time, Jin Baoxian, director of the city-run public bus management office, took five or six drivers to persuade them to stop, and the verbal conflict led to a fight. Chen, a driver on the side of the city-run public bus, and Hu Jinpu were beaten on the spot and could not walk, and were immediately sent to the hospital for emergency treatment. The lives of the two were in great danger. Director Jin Baoxian suffered a serious head injury. On the side of the private Chinese public bus, ticket seller Fan Gongyu suffered a serious head injury with a knife mark seven inches long, and his life may be in danger. Ticket checker Bao Shilin suffered a serious back injury. Ticket checker Liang Guoming injured his eyes, hands and feet. Ticket checker Chen Xiaoping suffered a broken leg. Six or seven drivers suffered minor injuries. The area, which is a necessary route through the central area, was in chaos for half an hour. A large number of police officers were dispatched by the Public Security Bureau to suppress the situation before it was calmed down. However, the drivers on both sides were still angry.

Second Tragedy: Although the first tragedy was suppressed by the police, the remaining anger of the drivers on both sides did not subside. More than 20 drivers of the private Chinese bus company took a bus and stopped two city-run public buses near East Sports Road, dragging the drivers and ticket sellers down and beating them severely. For a time, the passengers on the bus jumped out of the bus to escape, resulting in many people with abrasions. Later, city-run public bus No. 1023 caught up from behind, and the driver and ticket seller also got off to help, resulting in more and more people gathering and fighting each other. Fortunately, the security team of the Games heard the alarm and rushed to the scene, and then they all dispersed. It is reported that ticket sellers No. 123 and No. 152 of the city-run public bus management were seriously injured, and driver Wang Amao was also injured in the waist, and his life was also in danger. The responsible personnel immediately sent them to Tongren Hospital for treatment by ambulance.

Attitude of the Authorities: The authorities of the Games paid close attention to the two fights between the drivers of both sides, which led to a tragedy involving human lives. It is reported that the cause of the accident will be thoroughly investigated and dealt with strictly.

Dada Shipping Company Held its Annual Shareholders' Meeting Yesterday 126

Surplus of 140,000 to Expand Company Business, Zhang Xiaoru Died, Du Yuesheng Concurrently General Manager

This port's Dada Shipping Company held its annual shareholders' meeting at 2 pm yesterday at the Huzhou Guildhall on Guizhou Road. More than half of the shareholders attended the meeting. Du Yuesheng was elected chairman and reported on the business overview of the 23rd year and the future expansion plan. The details are recorded by the Riri News reporter as follows:

Business Overview: After the meeting was held as scheduled, there was a three-minute silence for the former general manager Zhang Xiaoru, who died, to express condolences. Then, Chairman Du Yuesheng reported on the business overview of the 23rd year, saying that the business this year was affected by the decline of the countryside and the depression of all industries. Between spring and summer, passengers and goods were unusually light, and there was no certainty in the business at the beginning. Fortunately, since the summer, wheat has been harvested and the source has surged. The company's original ships were insufficient to allocate, and it had to rent Jiahe, Jiangjing and other Jianglun ships to meet the urgent need. In autumn and winter, the business was smooth. Although the annual freight revenue was slightly higher than the previous year, it was impossible to obtain practical results due to the large expenses such as ship rental, coal consumption and night work. In terms of passenger transport, the revenue was also slightly higher than the previous year due to the improvement of passenger treatment, the elimination of the bad habits of the tea room, and the creation of the Hu Qing route by Datong Small Wheels and the implementation of the Shanghai Qing Intermodal Transport. Although the annual settlement obtained a surplus of more than 140,000 yuan, the occurrence of the third party's disturbance throughout the year was fortunate to have survived the difficulties. However, the future is still long, and the hidden worries have not ended. It still requires our efforts.

Improvement Plan: Then, Deputy Manager Yang Guanbei reported on the process of building the new Dada ship (omitted) and the future improvement plan. (1) In order to respect the intention of the Navigation Administration Bureau of the Ministry of Communications to create a model route for the Shanghai Yang route, our company will eliminate all kinds of bad habits on the ship and increase equipment to facilitate passengers. The measures that have been implemented include collecting 20% of the ticket price for silk tea room requests and wine fees, and the company will sell the berths in the unified cabin to eliminate the bad habits of the tea room monopolizing the berths. Other improvements, such as improving sanitary facilities and maintaining order, are gradually being implemented. (2) In the past two years, our company has been almost unable to cope with the occurrence of the third party. One wave has just passed halfway, and another wave has risen. Fortunately, none of them have been realized. However, the future is not optimistic. (3) Datong Wheel Bureau, jointly established by our company and Datong Company, has created Shanghai Qing Intermodal Transport. In the past year, the scale has been roughly established. Recently, Xinyun Company has opened the Zhen Qing route and the Beijing Shanghai Railway has implemented cargo intermodal transport, and price competition should not be underestimated. We are currently planning methods to resist and reduce the impact. (4) The company's ships start from Shanghai, and their final destination is Huo Jiaqiao in Yangzhou. Upstream, all the passengers and goods in the canal and the downstream river are handled by the Boluan Branch and the Gaoyou Shunhe Transport Company. Passengers and goods have always been transported by civilian ships, which are not economical in terms of time and money. In order to meet the needs of modern trends and facilitate merchants, our company established Datong Wheel Bureau and opened the Ning Qing shuttle, which is connected to the general company's ships. Since its implementation, merchants in Jiangbei have praised it. However, the Gaoyou Shaobo branches believed that the establishment of Datong's direct passenger and cargo traffic hindered their business. Gaoyou Zhihe and Datong Gaoyou Branch jointly resisted and refused Datong Small Wheels to dock at the wharf, causing a disturbance. Later, Chairman Wang of the Gaoyou Chamber of Commerce took the initiative to mediate, and the two companies evaluated and recovered the Shunhe and Datong Branch barges, Datong 30,000 yuan, Dada 20,000 yuan, and signed a contract to recover and self-operate. (5) Shaobo Branch repeatedly requested the company to recover and self-operate due to the difficulty in dividing the business scope due to the establishment of Datong. After many discussions, a false agreement was recently established to change it to the Huo Shao Bureau, and the business was merged, and the profits and losses were distributed according to the composition. From then on, all branches from Huoqiao to Qingjiang will be directly operated by the company, and the power will be unified and easy to manage. (6) In order to facilitate merchants and develop business, our company has established that the goods from Yaowan, Suqian, Bengbu and other places can be mortgaged to the bank with a bill of lading. In the future, we plan to extend it to Yancheng, Dongtai, Funing and other places, which is being planned.

Distribution of Profits: Supervisor Du Shaoru reported the accounts briefly, and then began to discuss the proposals. The board of directors proposed that the surplus of 148,516 yuan, 8 jiao, 3 fen and 9 li in the 23rd year, in addition to the statutory reserve, bonus and 1% dividend, the remaining funds should be used to reduce the cost of new ships. However, the proposed 1% dividend is now due to the company's addition of new ships and construction of warehouses, and there is a shortage of cash. It is proposed to pay 5 li first, and the remaining 5 li will be paid when the company's finances are abundant in the future. Please make a public decision on the case. It was resolved that a dividend of 1% should be paid, and the board of directors should find a way to clear it before the end of the lunar year.

Du Appointed General Manager: The general manager of Dada Company was originally Zhang Xiaoru. Zhang died in an accident a few days ago. Yesterday, the person in charge of the company told the Riri News reporter that the board of directors had appointed Chairman Du Yuesheng to concurrently serve as the general manager. In the future, the company's business will be further developed. Deputy Manager Yang Guanbei and Supervisors Du Shaoru and Zhang Weici were re-elected after the election, it is said.

Blind Children's and Mute Schools Celebrate Achievements with Art Exhibition 127

Wonderful Performance Items, Finally Seeing the Disabled but Not Useless

Shanghai Blind Children's and Mute Schools at No. 290 Hongqiao Road, West Shanghai, has been established for more than ten years and has achieved outstanding results. It is a leader in special education in China. The school held an art exhibition and supplemented the graduation ceremony for blind students on the past two days. I was specially invited to visit and will record the grand occasion I saw below.

Guest Titles: It is estimated that Mrs. Wu, Zhu Shaoping, Yan Fuqing, Gui Yingsheng, Le Zhenbao, Wang Wanbai and other 500 people arrived the day before yesterday. Yesterday was Sunday, and thousands of people from all walks of life arrived, and students accounted for the majority. First, in the melodious music of the school's blind student band, we visited various workshops or performance exhibition rooms. The rattan displays of the blind school were colorful and beautiful. The mute shuttle paintings, sculptures, labor and other products were about a thousand pieces, exquisite and pleasing to the eye, which can be called a grand view.

Graduation Ceremony: It was held the day before yesterday afternoon. There were three blind students in the normal school and seven in the complete primary school. Mrs. Wu, the chairman of the board of directors of the Fuya School, personally gave the certificates. The blind students bowed and received the certificates, and retired after saluting. Their movements were lively, just like ordinary people. Then, Guo Zengtong, a graduate, gave a reply. He spoke English first and then Mandarin. His words were sincere and his tone was loud. The sound of praise from the guests filled the audience.

Artistic Performance: There were more than ten programs, among which the performances were skillful, wonderful and moving, such as the four-tone ensemble and piano solo by blind students. The rise and fall of the tone and the harmony were harmonious. The blind students piled up Luohan, sometimes like a tall building, sometimes forming a high tower. The movements were lively and the style was novel, which was truly commendable. The dumb students' performance was clear and audible, and the results were surprisingly amazing. During the performance, a dumb student first used hand gestures and other movements to express his will. The guests all understood the magic. Then, another dumb student translated the student's movements into words on the blackboard, and then a dumb student read them out in a loud voice. Although the tone was light and turbid and slightly indistinguishable, it was also clear and audible.

Hand-written Words: A teacher first taught the dumb students to use their fingers to bend and stretch to make dumb literary gestures, and the students immediately wrote a long English sentence on the blackboard with a pen, and then translated it into Chinese. The words and meanings were quite impressive. Other dances by dumb girls, Tan Tui by dumb boys, and the blind playing the piano to harmonize with the rhythm were all in sync, humorous and funny, which won a lot of applause. People who are blind and dumb have already suffered from disability and uselessness. Now, with the power of education, the blind can read and the dumb can speak, and they can also learn crafts and skills, turning disability into usefulness. The omnipotence of education is increasingly believed and confirmed here.

The New Life Training Class for Tea Room Staff of China Merchants Bureau, organized by the New Movement General Association, has been running for two months. However, tea room training is an unprecedented initiative in China and has attracted much attention from people from all walks of life. The organizational content and the graduation ceremony held by the class at 10 am the day before yesterday are recorded as follows:

Organizational Content: The class was established on August 20, with the school site at Huazhan, Pudong, and a total of 120 students. There is one director and one deputy director, director Song Zhenduo, and deputy director Qi Fuming. It is divided into three groups: Teaching Affairs, Training Affairs, and General Affairs. Song Zhenduo is the head of the Teaching Affairs Office, Jiang Jingrong is the head of the General Affairs Group, and Song Chongli is the head of the Training Group. The subjects include: (1) Common Sense of Civics, (2) Common Sense of Service, (3) Spiritual Admonitions, (4) Military Training, (5) New Movement Theory, (6) Party Principles, (7) History and Geography, (8) Hygiene, (9) Mandarin. There are a total of nine subjects, and the management and teaching are particularly serious. After three months of strict training, the general knowledge of tea room staff has gradually increased, and their thinking has also been improved, which is truly commendable.

Guest Titles: Yesterday was the expiration of the first training period of the class. A graduation ceremony was specially held in the school's auditorium. The venue was newly decorated, and many guests from various agencies participated. There were Yan Baohang, representative of the New Movement General Association, Peng Hu, representative of the Ministry of Communications, Shi Zhonggang, special commissioner of the Chinese Seamen's Party Affairs, Wang Ya, representative of the Chinese Seamen's Union Special Commissioner's Office, Zhang Yaoming, representative of the Shanghai Branch of the Seamen's Union, Shao Xubai, representative of the General Labor Union, Lin Xueyan, representative of the Public Security Bureau, and dozens of representatives from various departments of the China Merchants Bureau. The gathering was a grand event for a while.

Then they entered the seats in an orderly manner. The opening order was as follows: (1) Stand at attention, (2) Sing the Party Song, (3) Bow to the Party-State flag and the portrait of the General President, (4) Read the President's Will, (5) , (6) Speeches by various guests, (7) Reply by the trainees, (8) Award Graduation Certificates, (9) Sing the New Movement Song, (10) Finish.

Chairman's Admonition: After Chairman Song Zhenfeng performed the rituals, he gave an impromptu speech, saying that the class was established on August 20 and has been in session for two months. The training is now complete and they will soon return to serve on the ships. People in the community recognized that the long-standing bad system of tea rooms was about to be reformed. However, when you were first transferred ashore, there were many rumors. Some said that the China Merchants Bureau was using the new life movement to transfer workers in order to lay off workers, and some said that they were drawing blood when inspecting their bodies, and now the workers are all pale and thin. These rumors disrupt the sight and hearing. Now, not only have workers not been laid off, but all workers are healthier than before. There are already facts to answer, so there is no need to say more. In the past, you yourselves thought that the status of tea room staff was humble, and you had no progressive thoughts and no polite behavior. Even when you first came to this class, you had this attitude. After two months of short-term training, your behavior and politeness have greatly improved. On the 9/18 Memorial Day, when we talked about the Dongsi provinces, you all shed tears. This is comforting. People have always thought that China's cultural level is too low and incurable. In you who have not received considerable education, your thoughts and behaviors have improved so much. In this post, I feel that China has great hope. Now that you are about to return to serve on the ships, you must maintain this spirit and fulfill some national obligations for the country. This is my hope.

Guest Speeches: First, Yan Baohang gave a speech, saying that he felt that the trainees were energetic and orderly, and the results were very satisfactory. The efforts and enthusiasm of the organizers and relevant groups have made this effect possible in such a short period of two months. Yesterday, I met Special Commissioner Yang, who also expressed great approval of the training of tea room staff. He had previously made a speech, hoping to continue the efforts and hoping that all private companies would also train workers, so that the Chinese shipping industry would be able to usher in a new era. Second, Peng Hu gave a speech, saying that if we can continue to work hard with this spirit, let alone revive the shipping industry, we will also rely on this to revive the Chinese nation. Wang Zhonggang gave a speech, saying that when he just arrived at the pier, he saw the well-trained marchers. He thought it was a military exercise. Only later did he know that it was the trained workers doing a military-style exercise. A group of disorderly workers, after a short period of training, became a well-organized team, which is really unprecedented. Zhang Yaoming gave a speech, saying that the enemy of China's labor movement is imperialism. Don't misunderstand the oppression of capital. We should cooperate between labor and capital to fight against the enemy imperialists. The rest of the speech was omitted. The meeting adjourned at 12 o'clock, it is said.

New Edition of Lai Gutang's Epistolary Letters Published: Sixth Volume of the Chinese Literature Rare Book Series 141

The Chinese Literature Rare Book Series published by the Shanghai Magazine Company has been releasing two volumes every Saturday since the 14th of this month, without interruption. This allows subscribers to feel as though they are subscribing to a Chinese literature weekly magazine. The ordinary method of subscribing, which entails paying first and then receiving the books later, further enhances the excitement. Yesterday marked the sixth week, and the publication released was "New Transcripts of Famous Scholars' Letters from Lai Gutang," compiled by Zhou Lianggong during the late Ming and early Qing dynasties. It contains the calligraphy of many prominent figures from the late Ming Dynasty, representing a collection of letters. It was banned after the Qing Dynasty, and the entire book was destroyed. The value of letters that were disliked by the authorities is evident. Literary scholars cherished even a single excerpt, keeping it hidden away. During the Daoguang era, the Haishan Xianguan series reprinted it, but with many deletions, alterations, and revisions. This series is printed based on the original Lai Gutang edition, totaling over 120 pages and containing over 700 letters. Its meticulous editing and the light and graceful style of the writing make it a top-tier collection of letters. It is essential reading for those who love late Ming literature and relish reciting correspondence. Zhang Jinglu has proofread and annotated the book. Another collection, "A Collection of Unusual Neighboring Affairs," is reportedly also slated for inclusion in the series. The retail price for the popular edition is 50 cents, while the special edition is 70 cents. Mail orders from outside Shanghai are exempt from postage. The deadline for subscribing to the first series of books is the end of this month, with only ten days remaining. The popular edition costs only 17 yuan, while the special edition costs only 24 yuan. Payments can be made in installments, with monthly payments of just three to four yuan to acquire the entire series. Next week's release will be "The Golden Lotus." In response to reader demand, the third volume is being rushed into print and will be available as early as Thursday. The retail price for all five volumes is 1.50 yuan. Individual subscriptions are available for just 1.10 yuan, with the special edition priced at 1.60 yuan. There is also a large, exquisitely bound hardcover edition with a colored spine and gold stamping, priced at 1.50 yuan, but available for subscription at only 2 yuan. It is both beautiful and magnificent.

Letter to the Editor 144

Respectfully, I have read today's issue of your newspaper regarding the Longzi case of Lu Xihou's false accusation of forging private documents and the details of the trial. As for what was recorded, at the time, accountant Li Ding specifically came to visit and persuade me to compromise, allowing the huge sum of two hundred seventy-eight thousand to be declared as a claim, and Lu would withdraw the accusation against me. I refused firmly, etc. This differs slightly from Longzi's original statement that accountant Li Ding came to visit and talk about the recent resolution of the Shanghai branch of the Chinese Industrial Bank, going to the liquidator and asking the liquidator to persuade me to compromise and allow the huge sum of one hundred seventy-eight thousand (that is, the 150,000 yuan of the Qunyi Syndicate capital taken over by Lu Xihou, who also had relatives and friends vouch in court that they would not claim debts during the liquidation period, about 123,000 yuan) to be declared as a claim, while Lu Xihou submitted a statement to the court declaring an error and withdrawing his own private statement. After the first creditors' meeting, Lu Xihou also intended to propose a new plan to pay 50%, but also asked the court to allow him to declare the aforementioned debt amount. The recent cause of the false accusation clearly arose from the failure to fulfill the request to declare the debt. I want to know that I can forgo being a judge, but I will never violate the law, etc. The slight discrepancy is probably because when Longzi made his statement, he was agitated and spoke quickly, and the reporter could not record everything, leading to this error. I hereby request a correction to clarify this. Sincerely, Yu Changzi, October 20th, 10 AM.

Snippets 145

— (Drunken Woodcutter)

Conscience is like a mirror, but it is sometimes covered with dust, losing its original luster. When we look at it and find that the mirror is blurry, reflecting a dim image, we must wipe it clean with a dry cloth, and then the radiance of the face will appear. That is the day when a person's conscience is tormented, repents, and renews itself.

Indeed, one cannot see one's own face clearly, so by looking in a mirror, one can clearly see one's own image. I am angry, I am happy, but when I put down the mirror, I no longer recognize myself. Therefore, there are many sinful people in society, with ferocious faces, doing things that are harmful and contrary to reason, without realizing it. This is all because they refuse to look in the mirror, or even do not know what a mirror is! However, their fate is to not escape the net of the law, thus forming a clear precedent for society.

Although a huge mirror hangs high in society, people seem to be blind, unable to see it. Thus, the tide of evil in society is surging!

Young people: on the road we are taking, each of us must hold a mirror, constantly looking at it, so that we will not have regrets for stumbling.

Such is Shanghai 146

— Zhu Ying

I recently saw an article in the Australian Victorian Daily, written by Mr. Laurie Aro, who had lived in Shanghai for many years. In it, as he was taking leave to return to Australia, he gives Shanghai a true portrayal.

He says:!

In films and novels, "the Paris of the Huangpu River" is often portrayed as an incredible city, full of luxury, wealth, debauchery, and even tropical flavors. These depictions can startle those who have been to Shanghai. Perhaps these are still impressions from the age of sailing ships, obtained by travelers far from Shanghai.

Modern Shanghai is not the Shanghai of films, novels, or dramas. Shanghai is cleaner than London, and life in Shanghai is not as luxurious as commonly said; it is cheaper than London and New York. Why does everyone say that the cost of living in Shanghai is terrifyingly high? I think that most returning overseas Chinese save up some money before returning home, and during their vacations, they still receive their salaries, so they put on a lavish display, which causes misunderstandings among the general public.

In Shanghai, finding a job these days is not easy. Although a small number of overseas Chinese drift to Shanghai and find jobs, most overseas Chinese are dejected, silent, and leave Shanghai.

Many films and novels portray Shanghai with suggestive backdrops. This is truly a joke. The climate of Shanghai is extremely lovable. Although Shanghai has cold winters and hot summers, the climate from October to December is so good that it can be said that no major city in the world can compare.

A Situation That Cannot Be Ignored! 149

Xuezi 150

— Gao Ji'an

I remember last autumn, on the ferry crossing the Moji Strait on my way from Nagasaki to Tokyo, I met a movie star from Kyoto. Her name was Nakajima Yukiko, though she didn't tell me her real name. With a long face and a slender figure, she was a thoroughly Westernized beauty.

Having a woman in the same car made the long train ride to Tokyo very talkative. We talked about everything, past and present, Chinese and foreign. She told me that she was from Tokyo, that her father was a businessman, and that her mother had already died. Her father was still in Tokyo, and this time because her father was ill, she had specially given up filming on location in Unzen to rush back to visit him.

My hopes are all dashed. I only love my old mother. My father is okay too, but he's an alcoholic. He's only loyal to his business. He doesn't seem to miss me much. When my mother was alive, she loved me very much, but she's dead. The house in Tokyo is also eerily quiet, because I love movies, so I also live in Kyoto… Mr. Gao! Do you still have your parents?

"I have both, and they are both well."

"People with mothers are so happy. Are you going to see your mother when you return from Tokyo this time?"

"Of course. She's missing her son who's traveling abroad."

On the road with autumn yellow leaves, the train ran very quickly on the Tokaido Main Line. Passing Osaka, she pointed to the Osaka station and said again: "Next to Osaka there is a place called Takarazuka. Mother is from there. There's not a day that I don't miss her."

She was also very knowledgeable in literature. She was very familiar with Mushanokoji Saneatsu, Kikuchi Kan, etc. We talked very congenially. I tried my best to comfort her about her loss of her mother. Indeed, the Japanese ideal of a good wife and wise mother is worth the eternal remembrance of women.

Afterwards, in Tokyo, she also came to the Imperial Hotel to see me. It was said that her father's illness had also improved. She invited me to play, so I also spared some time from my busy schedule to go to Nikko with her once. The next day she returned to Kyoto and told me to stay in Kyoto for a while on my way back.

Because Tokyo was really annoying, things were always settled in geisha houses after drinking. I was tired of eating raw fish, and the jade garden of famous wine and First Love History gave me a slight relief with its pine aroma, but I left immediately. When the car arrived in Yokohama, I telegraphed ahead. The next morning, when the Fuji Limited Express train entered Kyoto Station, Yukiko was already waiting for me and immediately asked me to go to her house. There was no way, I had to obey. The first thing she did after arriving home was to show me a photo of her and her mother.

Two days later I left and made an appointment to see her again, and also told her my Shanghai address. After returning, we occasionally exchanged a few letters.

Cool autumn has come to the world again. On a desolate winter night, Yukiko must be missing her mother again!

Records of Royal Incense Vaguely Floating 152

Although she did not sing triumphantly, there was indeed a faint, trembling melody in her voice; only because heaven had given her such a transcendent position, she dared not neglect her inherent dignity at any time and place, and even lost the freedom to sing, otherwise I think she would definitely hum a tune in the bathtub!

Whereabouts

Trip to Nanchang 153

— Tu Xiaochao

I traveled to Jiangxi, Hunan, Hubei, etc. in late summer and early autumn, then turned back to Shanghai, passing through Wuning. My deepest impression was of the trip to Nanchang. Although Nanchang is the capital of Jiangxi Province, it is located in a remote inland corner. When I traveled there in the past, I felt that its streets were simple and crude, inferior to other cultural ports in the Yangtze River basin. In recent years, because Generalissimo Chiang Kai-shek was stationed in Nanchang for many years to suppress the Red bandits, the city's population suddenly increased, and commerce gradually prospered. In addition, the provincial government painstakingly managed and strived to improve municipal administration and transportation. The main highway lines in all directions of Jiangxi have long been completed. The Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway is also about to be single-tracked. All these roads take Nanchang as the hub. The railway passes through Nanchang, with a north and south station. The south station is magnificently built and will soon be completed. Nanchang's electricity and telephone services have long been properly reorganized and are extremely convenient to use. Tap water is also being planned and implemented, and it is planned to raise large sums of money to rebuild the scenic Tengwang Pavilion. In addition to building wide roads, Nanchang City has also opened up a new residential area in the north of the city, giving the city a new look. When I set foot here this time, I had a strong sense of the past and present!

In the past, I often felt that traveling in the interior of China was not only fraught with the dangers of difficult water and land transportation, but also that the hostels and restaurants where I stayed were cramped and the food was not to my liking. This kind of hardship in traveling was not unique to remote areas, and in the past, those who stayed in Nanchang were also quite worried about finding good food. This time when I was serving in Jiangxi Province, I also thought about the problem of accommodation and food. Later, in the ship and train car, I learned that Nanchang had recently established a Hongdu Guesthouse. It was said that the accommodation and food were very comfortable, so I went directly to the guesthouse and stayed for a few days. During these few days, it was beyond my expectations. The feeling of being uncomfortable with staying and eating in Nanchang was relieved, and I added a lot of fun to my travels.

I have lived in Shanghai for a long time and have been quite troubled by the noise and clamor. When I arrived at the guesthouse, I unpacked my luggage and immediately felt refreshed. The guesthouse is located in the middle section of Wang Yangming Road in the new residential area. The buildings are magnificent, the courtyards are spacious, the location is quiet, and the transportation is extremely convenient. Those who stay here always feel like they are in another world. They are happy with its elegance and free from the pain of hustle and bustle, which is why their mood is refreshed. In terms of equipment, it is no less than the major hotels in Shanghai. The Western and Chinese dishes are also exquisitely prepared, so many high-end travelers who come to Nanchang gather here. Because Nanchang's municipal administration has been updated and the food is more comfortable, I have a particularly deep impression of my trip to Nanchang, so I am writing this down.
